Britain, France, America, and Italy Disagree on Germany; Disarmament Almost Adjourned Until Next Year; France Insists on Original Agreement; Italy Proposes Adjournment; Britain and America Hope to Find New Plan; Soviet Russia Does Not Agree to Change Venue

(Geneva) This afternoon, a meeting will be held at the residence of League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, which may determine the future of the Disarmament Conference. A final decision will be made at the main committee meeting tomorrow. It is believed that there is no other way than to adjourn the meeting, so that those engaged in diplomatic talks have the opportunity to find a way to resolve this current difficulty. It is now said that representatives of the powers will meet with Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson in San Remo or another Italian city in early December to discuss it. Russian representative Dovgalevsky met with Henderson this morning and was heard to explain that the Russian government is prepared to continue to cooperate on disarmament work, especially the continuation of the Disarmament Conference, but the Soviet Union opposes moving the meeting elsewhere. (Reuters, 20th)

(Geneva) Unless the four-power representative meeting tomorrow can achieve results beyond human power and reach a unified plan, Disarmament Chairman Henderson will convene the main committee on Tuesday or Wednesday to propose that the General Committee, originally scheduled to reopen on December 4, be postponed until January next year, because it is expected that the atmosphere can be clarified through diplomatic negotiations at that time. However, if the General Committee does decide to postpone the meeting, it is believed that France will attempt to begin direct negotiations with Germany. At today's four-representative meeting, they still wanted to resolve their position on Germany. The four representatives of the United States, Britain, France, and Italy had tea and talked for three hours at Henderson's residence, discussing whether to use the declaration of British Foreign Secretary Simon on October 14 as the basis for continuing the meeting, or to find a new plan. However, no decision was made. It is heard that French representative Paul-Boncour insisted on the principles of the October 14 declaration as the basis for the convention, but the British and American representatives were willing to revise it, while the Italian representative advocated that the meeting wait and see for the time being, and it is expected that something can be decided after the meeting at League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol's villa next year. (National Dispatch, 19th)

(Geneva) The representatives of Britain, France, Italy, and the United States met for three hours today without results. Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson commented on the status of the Disarmament Conference, stating the need to obtain a greater common ground before the British draft convention is submitted for second reading. After the meeting adjourned, although the countries remained silent, it is known that this meeting did not reach any resolution. The major powers have different positions on the procedures to be adopted in the future. French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour advocated continuing the Disarmament Conference on the one hand, and supported the MacDonald revised plan agreed upon on October 14 on the other. It is heard that the United States also agrees to continue the meeting, but feels that the United States is not bound by the October 14 agreement. If an agreement can be obtained by other methods, the U.S. government will not cease cooperation. As for Italy, it clearly expressed its proposal for adjournment. Britain now feels that the agreement of October 14 has failed to achieve an understanding. It is heard that after tomorrow's four-power meeting, the main committee meeting will be held on Tuesday. It is believed that the General Committee will adjourn from December 4 to January 4. The proposal is likely to be realized. (Reuters, 19th)

(Geneva) The main representatives met at Henderson's residence today for three hours. The general impression is that Chairman Henderson is very eager for the Disarmament Conference to continue its work. As for the other representatives, they merely reiterated the opinions they had expressed during yesterday's talks. The British representative argued vehemently the reasons why the government was seeking a new basis for discussion in order to save the Disarmament Conference. The Italian representative advised postponement, saying that concluding a disarmament convention at a time when Germany had withdrawn from the meeting would be in vain. U.S. delegation chairman Davis was not in Geneva, and his representative (namely the minister to Switzerland Wilson) merely reiterated Davis's recent declaration, saying that from now on, disarmament is only a matter concerning Europe. General Rapporteur Bellus remained silent. French representative Paul-Boncour declared in a very firm tone that the French government insisted on the principles decided on October 14 based on British suggestions. Paul-Boncour said that France had made concessions to the extreme and could not concede any further. The French representative's declaration shocked the representatives present, and British Foreign Secretary Simon has realized from this point on that it would be futile for Britain to propose a new basis for discussion. In this situation, what will the future of the Disarmament Conference be? Judging from the situation on all sides, it seems that the Disarmament Conference may either be postponed or continue on the basis of the Simon presentation of October 14. This will be considered starting tonight. It is estimated that the Italian delegation will advocate postponement and will obtain the support of the British and American delegations. The General Committee of the Disarmament Conference, originally scheduled to meet on December 4, will be changed to meet in January next year. The French representative opposes this postponement, saying that a disarmament convention must be concluded and that it is possible to conclude one. The French representative does not want to bear the responsibility for the postponement of the meeting and Henderson's resignation, believing that the consequences would be unimaginable if Mr. Henderson were to resign. The Disarmament Conference presidium will probably convene on Tuesday to make it clear to them the proposals of the major countries. In exceptional cases, the meeting will be open. Before the meeting at Henderson's residence today, Paul-Boncour and Bellus had a long talk, and the two had a detailed observation of the situation. (Havas, 19th)

(Geneva) German newspapers reported news from Geneva that British Foreign Secretary Simon's deputy Eden intends to visit Italian Prime Minister Mussolini in Rome because the Disarmament Conference is completely hopeless, in order to find a way to break the deadlock. Public opinion believes that this is only a method of convening a meeting of the signatories of the Four-Power Pact. (National Dispatch, 20th)

French New Cruiser Launched; 17,600 Tons Displacement

(Paris) A French new cruiser was launched today at the Brest Naval Shipyard. The ship is the first of six identical cruisers under construction to be completed, displacing 17,600 tons, travelling at 32.5 nautical miles per hour, and mounting nine 6-inch caliber guns. (National Dispatch, 19th)

Romanian Political Tide; France States It Did Not Interfere

Bucharest, Romanian Capital: Since the resignation of the Vanda Cabinet and the succession of Liberal Party leader Duca as Prime Minister, newspapers of the extreme nationalist faction have subtly implied that the development of the Romanian political situation has a lot to do with the potential influence of the French government. Foreign Minister Titulescu today met with French Minister Tommaso on this propaganda. After the meeting, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued a communique stating that the French Minister stated that the French government never interferes in the internal affairs of other countries, and that it has nothing to do with the recent Romanian cabinet tide. Foreign Minister Titulescu said that what Tommaso said is true, and that the French government has no partiality towards Romanian political parties. (Havas, 19th)

Spain's General Election: Right-Wing Parties Achieve Complete Victory; Women Exercise Suffrage for the First Time; Scattered Riots and Strikes Occur

Madrid – A special edition of the newspaper was issued today, announcing that the right-wing parties have achieved a complete victory in the election. Rumors circulate that the Socialist Party is preparing a large demonstration. (Reuters, 20th)

Madrid – Initial reports from the Spanish general election indicate that right-wing parties hold a dominant position, having secured 150 seats. The Socialist Party has only obtained 110 seats thus far, seemingly losing 60 seats. Leaders of the right-wing parties anticipate securing approximately 200 seats in the parliament. (National Telegram, 20th)

Madrid – In this election, 70 candidates from 44 parties are vying for the 470 seats in the parliament. Currently, each party claims victory. What is known is that the right-wing parties hold a slight advantage over the Socialist Party. The failure of the Radical Party foreshadows the downfall of the Barrios government. A second round of voting is required in 35 out of 45 provinces because candidates must secure 40% of the votes to be elected. In Madrid, the forces of the right-wing parties and the Socialist Party are evenly matched. In Cadiz, Badajoz, and Avila, the Radical Party has suffered significant losses, with all seats being won by the right-wing parties. It is reported that Prime Minister Barrios was defeated by a leader of the Catholic Youth League in Seville province. In several provinces, right-wing and Radical Party candidates have formed alliances to oppose the Socialist Party, making the situation highly complex. The Catholic Party leader Robles has been elected. The Communist Party has also won in León and Madrid. The Catholic Party claims to have won in the capitals of 30 provinces, including Andalusia, a stronghold of the Socialist Party. Angered by their defeat, the Socialist Party blames female voters, threatening revolution and street fighting. It is noted that female voters outnumber male voters by 5%, and they mostly voted for right-wing candidates. (Reuters, 20th)

Madrid – According to unofficial vote count reports at 1:00 AM this morning in the Spanish general election, popular sentiment is leaning towards the right wing. The Radical Party leader and incumbent Prime Minister Barrios suffered a crushing defeat. Barrios ran as a candidate in Seville but was defeated by a young professor named Bafang by approximately 9,000 votes. In most other provinces, right-wing candidates also emerged victorious. According to People's Party leader Robles, the right wing is assured of 180 seats in the new parliament. This election was relatively peaceful, arguably the least conflict-ridden since Spain became a republic. Only three people died. Voter turnout was very high throughout the country, approximately 80-90%. This was the first time women had the right to vote, which further boosted turnout. In many places, the number of votes cast by women was often three times that of men. (National Telegram, 20th)

Madrid – The first general election since the establishment of the Spanish Republic was held today. Reports of strikes and violence are emerging from various locations. Voting commenced nationwide at 9:00 AM this morning. Initial reports from 16 provinces, including former strongholds of the Socialist Party and the extreme left wing, indicate a right-wing victory. However, due to the complexity of the electoral system, a definitive result cannot be estimated until tomorrow. Women are exercising their right to vote for the first time, numbering approximately eight million. Determined to eradicate unrest, their voter turnout far exceeds that of men. The streets of Madrid are thronged with people. Churches are filled with Catholics praying for a favorable outcome. Many women walk in groups, rosaries in hand. One female teacher stood outside a polling station all night, hoping to cast the first female vote. Many nuns and disabled individuals also joined the crowds to vote. It is estimated that half of the electorate had voted within the first two hours. The crowds are jubilant, but the police are heavily guarded. Machine guns are positioned on major streets, and police cars and mounted police patrol back and forth. The order in the capital is relatively good, but disturbances have occurred in many provinces, particularly in Seville and Torrent, where clashes between socialists and the right wing resulted in two deaths and several injuries. In Palma de Mallorca, a bomb exploded, damaging tram tracks and the entrance to a tram depot, causing all trams to be withdrawn. Throughout the day today, troops are stationed at the Bank of Spain headquarters, gas plants, and other public places to provide strict protection. Transportation workers in Barcelona are on strike, hindering travel. It is reported that relatives of former dictator Primo de Rivera have been arrested there. There are also reports of an assassination attempt on the mayor of Puerto Real. (Reuters, 19th)

Mussolini Emphasizes Agriculture; Protects Farmers, Increases Wheat Production

Rome – The Italian government is currently undertaking a plan to protect farmers and increase domestic wheat production. New regulations regarding the export of flour byproducts have been included in newly promulgated laws and are quite detailed. Furthermore, the proportion of domestic wheat that must be used in flour mills has also been established as law. Farmers across the country have largely followed Prime Minister Mussolini's initiated wheat campaign, investing heavily in expanding wheat cultivation, purchasing machinery, and engaging in new ventures, while receiving comprehensive protection from the government. (National Telegram, 20th)

Japan Conducts Mass Arrest of Communists; Over a Thousand Reported

(Tokyo) – The National Council of Japanese Labor Unions, which, under the guidance of red labor organizations and in cooperation with the Japanese Communist Party, continued to engage in bold struggles centered around various factories, suffered a collapse after its members, including Mizogami, Kakuda, Ito, Tanaka, and Ito Ichiro, were arrested in April last year. Only the cadres of the council remained. Later, they attempted to rebuild and expand their influence. The Labor Section of the Police Bureau, in consultation with the Ministry of Interior and the Tokyo District Public Prosecutors Office, notified various newspapers to prohibit the publication of related articles. On February 27 of this year, a large-scale search was conducted by the central authorities, and all members were arrested. This process has continued recently and is now coming to an end. The ban on news coverage was lifted at 5:00 PM on the 20th. The total number of people arrested in this operation is estimated to reach 1,696 (including 68 women and 926 Koreans). 145 people have already been indicted, making this a large-scale arrest unprecedented in modern times. (Japan United Press Telegram, 20th)

Death of Italian Politician Scialoja

Rome – Renowned Italian international law scholar and politician Vittorio Scialoja has passed away at the age of seventy-seven. Throughout his life, he wrote extensively on social, political, diplomatic, and colonial issues. He made particular contributions to the field of Roman law. He served as a senator from 1904, introducing many legal reforms. He held positions as Minister of Justice and Foreign Minister and served as Italy's representative to the League of Nations and peace conferences for many years. In March and September 1929, he served as Chairman of the League of Nations Council and Assembly. (Reuters, 20th)

Japan Expands Shenyang Arsenal, Attaches Chemical Warfare Weapons Manufacturing Plant, and Establishes Offices in Important Areas

Shenyang dispatch: Since the Soviet Union published the documents revealing Japan's conspiracy regarding the Eastern Railway, the Japanese side has deeply felt that the conflict has become acute. The Kwantung Army is actively engaged in deploying military equipment. In addition to mobilizing elite troops and transporting them to northern Manchuria, it is also greatly expanding the Shenyang Arsenal and establishing machinery repair offices in militarily important areas. These offices are located wherever troops are stationed. Their responsibilities include: (1) Japanese troops stationed in "Manchuria" are all under the control of the Kwantung Army, and all weapons are stored, repaired, and distributed by the Shenyang Arsenal (the offices are auxiliary repair facilities). (2) Except for a small number of simple repairs that can be done at the Shenyang Arsenal, the large-scale manufacturing is all done by the various ordnance factories in Japan. The parts are then shipped to the Shenyang Arsenal for assembly and distribution. (3) The Shenyang Arsenal is responsible for the above-mentioned missions. Its warehouses are fully stocked and specially guarded. At the same time, to prevent delays in military use, small warehouses and small repair shops are set up under the offices in important locations throughout "Manchuria." These are under the special protection of the local garrison and are given special treatment during wartime. (4) New facilities are being built to replace the existing buildings that are not suitable for weapon warehouses, and construction has already begun. (5) To supplement the national ordnance manufacturing efforts, the Shenyang Arsenal has attached a chemical warfare weapons manufacturing plant to its pharmaceutical factory, which serves as a supply depot for the chemical warfare unit. Part of the factory is being borrowed from other facilities, and part is under construction. (6) The well-known Kurume tank unit of Japan moved to Gongzhuling in early October. The Shenyang Arsenal has acquired an additional batch of work, and is currently assembling parts for them.

Chen Jitang's Attitude During the Fujian Incident: Not Involved in Fujian Turmoil; Another Reason for Li Xiang's Dismissal

Guangzhou dispatch: Since the events in Fujian Province unfolded, the situation in the southwestern provinces has become increasingly tense. Chen Jitang of Guangdong Province, carefully observing the internal and external situations, believes that recuperation and rest are best. Therefore, Chen Mingshu and others held repeated meetings in Hong Kong, but he adopted a non-committal attitude. At the same time, he adopted a policy of strict prevention militarily. Until recently, Chen Mingshu and others made more overt expressions, and Chen Jitang took decisive measures, stripping the military authority from Li Yangjing, commander of the Third Army, and Xiang Hanping, commander of the Second Army, because he suspected that Li and Xiang were colluding with Fujian. Chen Jitang now holds the military authority of the two armies himself. Li's resignation as commander of the Third Army has also been approved. Furthermore, Ouyang Xin, deputy commander of the 8th Division of the Third Army, has been appointed as the chief of staff of the Third Army. Ye Shouchao, commander of the 22nd Regiment of the 8th Division, has been promoted to deputy commander of the 8th Division. Deng Qinglin, director of the Third Army's Logistics Department and concurrently director of the Rear Affairs Office of the army, has also been dismissed. Jian Zuozhen has been appointed to replace him. As for the resigned officers of the Second Army, Chen Jitang has also appointed other personnel to replace them. With Li Xiang removed from his military power, the recent situation in Guangdong will not be affected by the independence of Fujian Province. At the same time, Chen Jitang is actively using former Fourth Army (Zhang Fakui's troops) officers, such as Miao Peinan, who is appointed as the chief of staff of the headquarters and concurrently the director of the training division. Li Hanhun and Deng Longguang also each command a division. Recently, Zhu Huiri returned to Guangdong, and there is news that he has been appointed as the chief advisor of the headquarters. This new army is no less than Chen Jitang's reserve force. Its troops are concentrated in Beijiang, Xijiang, the provincial capital, and Huizhou in Dongjiang. Yu Hanmou, commander of the First Army, has also been stationed in the provincial capital since returning from southern Jiangxi. Therefore, from the current situation, Guangdong Province will not be involved in the Fujian Province turmoil. (November 16th)

Guangzhou Municipality Bans Rent Increases on Houses, Provincial Government Promulgates Measures to Ban Renting of Houses

Guangzhou dispatch: In recent years, Guangzhou City has continuously opened up roads, and the city's brokers have raised capital, specializing in industrial speculation and monopoly, resulting in the soaring rental values of houses in the city. Old-style houses are decreasing day by day, while newly built Western-style buildings are increasing day by day. An ordinary family of four cannot manage with a monthly rent of less than 20 or 30 yuan. If a family has six or seven members, they must pay a monthly rent of 50 or 60 yuan, causing housing panic among the middle and lower classes. Even renting a single room costs no less than ten yuan per month. The lament of "Chang'an is not easy to live in" is unexpectedly seen in Guangzhou today. Recently, the Municipal Council has repeatedly suggested on the rent issue, asking to restrict landlords from demanding high rents and asking the authorities to ban rent increases on houses to maintain the livelihood of the common people. It also requests to stipulate proper measures for guaranteeing rented houses. The authorities immediately gathered suggestions from various parties, drafted housing rental regulations, which were revised and passed by the provincial government and promulgated for implementation. The regulations were promulgated yesterday, and the appendix is as follows:

Article 1: These regulations apply to all houses in Guangzhou City used for residence or for residence and small industrial and commercial businesses. Article 2: Rent increases for the houses mentioned in the previous article shall be subject to the following provisions, but this does not apply if the lease contract specifically stipulates rent increase methods: (1) For newly built houses or houses purchased through sales that are rented out after the implementation of these regulations, rent increases are not allowed until five years have passed from the date of the lease. The amount of the rent increase shall not exceed 30% of the original rent. (2) For the period stipulated in the preceding paragraph, if the tenant changes during the period, the five-year period must continue to be satisfied according to the original lease date before the rent can be increased. (3) Before the implementation of these regulations, for all leased houses, if the five-year period has expired and the rent has not been increased, 30% of the original rent may be added. If the ten-year period has expired and the rent has not been increased, 60% of the original rent may be added. However, the basis of the original rent should be based on the police district register. Article 3: The landlord shall not demand any other fees from the tenant under any pretext other than the proper rent and the provisions of these regulations. Article 4: When the landlord rents out the house, he may collect one month's rent as a deposit from the tenant. When the tenant moves out, it can be deducted from the rent for the last month, but the tenant must notify the landlord in writing one month in advance before moving out. Article 5: When renting a house, the tenant must obtain a store's stamped guarantee according to custom, or pay the landlord two months' rent in advance as a guarantee. When moving out, if there are no rent arrears, the landlord shall return the full amount. Article 6: If the tenant commits any of the following circumstances, the landlord may apply to the police district office to order the tenant to move out and recover the rent owed: (1) Owes two months' rent and still does not pay the rent after the landlord's time-limited reminder. (2) Uses the house for illegal purposes for himself or others. (3) Transfers the house to others without the landlord's consent. Article 7: When the landlord sells the house or notifies the tenant of self-occupation or reconstruction, he should immediately go to the police district office to report the situation for the record, for future reference and for the convenience of clearing donations. Article 8: The landlord must notify the tenant to move out one month in advance when taking back the house. If he cannot move out when the deadline expires, the deadline should be extended by two months. However, this does not apply if there is a batch period stipulated. When the landlord takes back the house, he must compensate two months' rent for moving expenses, but the rent must be paid as usual during the moving period. If the tenant owes rent, it should be deducted from the compensation for moving expenses (November 11th)

Anti-Japanese Youths Petition for Living Relief: More Than 100 Participants; Chief Representative Yang Zhen Arrested

Beiping dispatch: After the fall of Northeast China, volunteer armies rose up to fight for national survival and fought bitterly in the icy and snowy wilderness for two years. Subsequently, after the signing of the Tanggu Truce, the volunteer armies were disbanded in essence, and many drifted to Beiping. Recently, Yang Zhen, a representative of the Overseas Chinese Volunteer Army, initiated the organization of the Anti-Japanese Youth League in Beiping, requesting the Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang Support Association to publish the accounts of anti-Japanese donations and to provide the remaining funds to maintain their livelihood. They had already submitted a report to the Municipal Party Headquarters, requesting approval for the organization, but there was no response. The Youth League then petitioned the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, and the Military Branch Office on the afternoon of the 17th. Chief Representative Yang Zhen was arrested on the way. More than 100 people, including youth, women, and children of the volunteer army, continued to wait at the Municipal Party Headquarters but to no avail. They continued to petition on the 18th. The details are recorded as follows:

Purpose of the Petition

Various anti-Japanese youths and their families, including women and children, stranded in Beiping took advantage of the City Consolidation Committee meeting on the afternoon of the 17th to petition the Municipal Party Headquarters. From 1:00 PM onwards, they gathered in front of the Municipal Party Headquarters, including more than 100 people from the troops of Su Bingwen, Ma Zhanshan, and others stranded in Beiping, as well as their families, women, children, and disabled persons. They requested three points: (1) Requesting strict orders for the Support Association to publish the accounts of income and expenditure of donations in the shortest possible time. (2) Requesting that the remaining amount of the Support Association's donations be handed over and fairly distributed by the Party and government authorities to resettle anti-Japanese comrades who are out of school and unemployed. (3) Requesting that living expenses for anti-Japanese comrades stranded in Beiping be provided during the petition. After the representatives gathered, they waited quietly for the chief representative, Yang Zhen, to arrive and proceed with the petition.

Representative Arrested

The representatives waited in front of the Municipal Party Headquarters for a long time. By 2:30 PM, Yang Zhen had not yet arrived. Later, it was reported that Yang Zhen had been arrested by military police on the way. Military police also went to Fozhao Tower to search Yang's residence, but found nothing. They only took away all the declarations that the league had printed but not yet distributed. It is reported that the reason for Yang Zhen's arrest, according to related parties, is that the Anti-Japanese Youth League in Beiping has not yet been approved by the authorities for registration and that the public gathering violated police regulations. Because there were many volunteer army officers and soldiers among them, the police did not arrest them, but the military police arrested Chief Representative Yang Zhen, and there were no major issues.

Party Headquarters Reply

The representatives gathered in front of the Municipal Party Headquarters. After hearing that Yang Zhen had been arrested, they immediately elected three representatives, Ren Dingsheng, Liu Jingbo, and Zhou Xueyong, to continue the petition to the Municipal Party Headquarters. Yang Bing, the secretary-general of the Municipal Party Headquarters, met with them. The representatives immediately stated the three points of the petition and said that the urgent task at present was to rescue Chief Representative Yang Zhen. Before Yang Zhen was released, all requests could be carried out later. Yang Bing said that the committee members were holding a meeting in Xihua Hall and that this issue could be brought to the committee members for instructions. The three representatives waited in the reception room, and the other representatives waited in front of the Municipal Party Headquarters. After the meeting in Xihua Hall ended at 5:30 PM, Yang Bing came out again to meet and told the representatives that the Municipal Party Headquarters had no power to release Yang Zhen and that it would be necessary to inquire with the Military Police Headquarters about the actual situation before deciding whether to provide assistance. The three representatives withdrew one after another, and the remaining representatives dispersed at 6:00 PM.

Second Petition

Anti-Japanese Youth League representatives Ms. Yin Binghun, Sun Han, Liu Jingbo, Ren Dingsheng, and Zhou Xueyong went to the Municipal Party Headquarters again at 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 18th to petition. Secretary-General Yang Bing was not there, and no one met with them. Ms. Yin and others then went to the Municipal Government. Mayor Yuan Liang sent Zhu Xingyuan to meet with them. The representatives stated the main points of the petition: (1) Requesting Mayor Yuan to order the immediate release of Yang Zhen. (2) Providing relief to anti-Japanese comrades stranded in Beiping. (3) Requesting the publication of the accounts of anti-Japanese donations. Zhu replied that he could convey the intentions of the gentlemen to the mayor and give a concrete answer next Tuesday. The five representatives then withdrew. (18th)

Liu Zhi Inspects Hua County, Advocates Resettling Disaster Victims in Special Zone, Provincial Government Sends Letters to Various Departments to Dispatch Personnel for Consultation

Kaifeng dispatch: Liu Zhi took a special train to Zhengzhou on the morning of the 15th and transferred to northern Henan for inspection. After crossing the river and arriving at the north bank at noon, he disembarked to inspect the dikes around Miaogong and the disaster situation in Wuzhi County. Wherever he went, he inquired about the hardships of the people. He transferred from Muluan Township to Zhan Township and boarded the special train north again. At 7:30 PM, he arrived at Daokou Township. Xie Suian, the magistrate of Hua County, and representatives from the commercial and academic circles of the town met with him. He spent the night in the train. On the morning of the 16th, Ren Bang, the magistrate of Jun County, and personnel from the county's Party headquarters met with him. Liu gave instructions on the reorganization of the Daokou Chamber of Commerce. Then, at 8:00 AM, he led Chen Ruzhen, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, to Hua County. After leaving the city, they switched to a small boat and visited the disaster areas of Baliying, Nanyangliu, Anshang Village, etc. The floodwaters had not receded and were still a vast expanse. The water flow at the Yellow River breach was very rapid, even greater than the downstream water势. Currently, there is no hope of cultivation. The disaster victims are scattered, separated from their families, crying from hunger and cold, a miserable sight. More than 10,000 people, supporting the old and carrying the young, prostrated themselves on the roadside begging for help. They returned to the city at 2:00 PM. He instructed Magistrate Xie to investigate the number of disaster victims capable of farming so that they could be given relief separately. At 4:30 PM, he returned to Daokou, and the special train departed at 6:30 PM. That night, it passed through Xinxiang and headed north. It is estimated that there are 300,000 disaster victims in Hua County, and their cries of suffering are everywhere, hoping for relief. Liu plans to have the government provide relief on the one hand and resettle some of the disaster victims in areas of southern Henan that have been devastated by the Red Bandits, where there is no smoke from cooking fires, so that they have land to cultivate and homes to live in. He has telegraphed the secretariat of the provincial government to send letters to various departments for consultation on how to proceed and to raise cotton clothes to keep the disaster victims warm, because the 17,000 sets allocated by the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association a few days ago are still not enough to distribute. The secretariat has sent letters to various departments to send personnel to gather at the provincial government at 2:00 PM this afternoon for consultation. (18th)

Kaocheng and Lanfeng Dike Closure Project Begins: First Build Earth Embankment with Sand Inside and Silt Outside; Approximately 4,000 Workers Employed at Two Locations

Kaifeng dispatch: The counties of Kaocheng and Lanfeng were the most severely affected by this year's Yellow River flood in Henan Province on the south bank. It is now winter, and the water level has dropped sharply. The First Engineering Office began working on closing the breaches in the middle of last month. To understand the true situation, the reporter visited the area a few days ago. The so-called Lanfeng breach refers to the southern end of Xiaoxin Dike. Reports of the breaches in Cailou Township, Tongwaxiang, and Zhenpu all refer to this. An earth embankment is now being built from the southern end of Xiaoxin Dike to the ancient road cliff about four li south to close the breach. It is eight meters wide at the base and three meters high, with sand inside and a one-meter-thick layer of silt outside. When construction began, there was still about a foot of water on the planned dike line. Earth-filled sacks were used to create a layer in the water, and then workers were instructed to take sand from the dry Yellow River channel to lay the dike base and the core. Each layer was packed with wooden or stone hammers to compact the soil. Then, silt was transported from the south bank of the old channel using iron-gauge carts on light-duty narrow-gauge railways and piled on both sides of the dike core. The built part is now about two meters high and has completed two-thirds of the entire dike project. The so-called Kaocheng dike breach refers to Yueti southwest of Renzhuang. Reports of the Simingtang breach and the Yuanzhai breach refer to this. A straight earth embankment is now being built from the Daxin Dike south of Yantan, directly connected to the levee behind Guying Village. The width, height, internal sand and external silt, and the use of wooden and stone hammer packing are the same as the Lanfeng project. Small carts are used to transport the sand and silt. It has now been built to a height of about 1.8 or 9 meters and has completed six-tenths of the entire dike project. According to engineers, both projects can be completed completely this year, with a total cost of about 60,000 yuan. However, because the dike with internal sand and external silt is not very solid, it may still collapse in the event of a flood. The agency responsible for guiding and supervising the project is the First Temporary District Engineering Office of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee. The office moved to Sanyizhai northwest of Lanfeng on October 10 and set up the First Works Office in Dinggantang Village, one li south of the old channel. The Second Works Office was set up outside the west gate of Simingtang, south of the Kaocheng dike breach. Each office has an engineer to guide the construction method and supervise the workers, as well as supervisors, general affairs, accounting, and other staff. The temporary engineering office has a radio station that reports the progress of work to the Gongzhen Group of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association on Dongerdao Street, Kaifeng, every day. The First Works Office in Lanfeng employs about 2,000 workers, and the Second Works Office in Kaocheng employs about 1,100 workers. The purpose is to provide relief through work. The wages for earthwork are six jiao per square ocean within 59 nanometers, and for those within 200 nanometers, the amount is increased according to the original fixed price. Later, due to the shortage of workers in Kaocheng, more than 800 people were recruited, and the total number of people at the two locations is now about 4,000, all of whom are disaster victims. Because their lives and property are at stake, the projects they are working on are very solid. However, the initial plan of the Water Conservancy Commission for the two projects called for an expenditure of 600,000 yuan and the use of reed rope, earth, stone, and other works to last a long time. Later, due to financial constraints, the current plan was revised, and the strength to protect the lives and property of the people in the two counties seems to be slightly weak. (18th)

Henan Province Distributes Clothing and Funds for Disaster Relief: 500,000 Disaster Victims in the Province; 37,000 Sets of Clothing; 100,000 Yuan in Temporary Relief Funds

Kaifeng Correspondence: This year, the Yellow River flooded, and Henan Province suffered particularly severe damage. Now that harsh winter has arrived, no fewer than 500,000 disaster victims are crying out for food and lack clothing to ward off the cold. The Henan Disaster Relief Committee, together with Yang Mingsheng, the Henan Investigation and Relief Director of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Group, repeatedly discussed and properly allocated clothing and funds to avoid the drawbacks of unfairness. A total of 37,000 sets of clothing were received in two installments and distributed as follows: 17,000 sets to Hua County, 3,500 sets to Fengqiu, 3,000 sets to Lanfeng, 3,000 sets to Kaocheng, 2,000 sets to Wuzhi, 2,000 sets to Wen County, 1,800 sets to Kaifeng, 1,000 sets to Sishui, 1,000 sets to Zheng County, 1,000 sets to Mengjin, 340 sets to Chenliu, 160 sets to Yucheng, and 120 sets to Meng County. There are still 1,080 sets remaining. At 2:00 PM yesterday, the Henan Disaster Relief Committee held its second meeting at the Civil Affairs Department. Those present included Li Peiji, Zhang Jingyu, Yang Mingsheng, Fang Qidao, and ten others. During the meeting, Yang Mingsheng proposed a plan for how to allocate the 100,000 yuan in temporary emergency relief funds allocated. It was decided that the standard would be to prioritize counties where disaster victims could not survive without relief. The counties with the most severe disasters were: Hua County (40,000 yuan), Lanfeng (10,000 yuan), Kaocheng (8,000 yuan), Wuzhi (6,500 yuan), Wen County (4,000 yuan), and Fengqiu (6,500 yuan). The next most severely affected counties were: Kaifeng, Mengjin, and Meng County (1,000 yuan each). The next most severely affected counties were: Guangwu, Sishui, Zhongmu, Minquan, Gong County, and Yucheng (500 yuan each). Other topics discussed included how to purchase grain for winter relief and how to establish reception centers for disaster victims in Kaifeng and Zhengzhou. Yang Mingsheng reported to the Disaster Relief Group on his recent investigation of the disaster situation in various counties and the emergency relief distribution situation, and requested instructions on handling winter relief in Henan. He took a train east to Shanghai tonight. (14th)

Resolution of Party-Government Dispute in Hubei Province: All Offensive Notices to Be Revoked; Provincial Government Sends Letter of Regret to Party Headquarters

Hankou Correspondence: The party-government dispute in Hubei Province has gradually been resolved through the mediation of Yu Xilai, the Central Kuomintang's inspector of party affairs in Hubei and Jiangxi provinces. The provincial government has now replied to the provincial party headquarters, revoking all notices offensive to the party headquarters and expressing regret. The provincial party headquarters did not pursue the matter further, and the case was resolved smoothly. As for Huang Danchu, the magistrate of Huangmei County, whose malfeasance and harm to the people have been confirmed, the Supervisory Yuan has already transferred him for disciplinary action, and the provincial government has no intention of condoning him. His dismissal from office is no longer a question. The provincial party headquarters believes that Huang was originally a party member and should be punished according to national law and party discipline. It was specifically resolved to submit the case to the Central Supervisory Committee for handling. The provincial government's official letter to the provincial party headquarters is recorded as follows: "In direct response, recently read your official letter instructing the Civil Affairs Department to withdraw Training Order No. 2725 and revoke all notices posted by its affiliated agencies, etc. Regarding this case, the Huangmei County Party Headquarters and various groups have previously sent repeated telegrams to the government, accusing Huang Danchu, the magistrate of the county. The government then transferred the matter to the Civil Affairs Department to send personnel to thoroughly investigate and report on the case as a basis for verification and handling. Subsequently, we received repeated orders from the Commander-in-Chief of the Encirclement and Suppression of Bandits in the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces to investigate and report. We previously submitted a document stating the situation and informed the Civil Affairs Department. This is the process by which the government handled this case. Yesterday, we read a newspaper report about the Public Security Bureau's Announcement No. 9. The government instructed the department to investigate and report. According to Director Meng of the Civil Affairs Department, the department received instructions from Your Excellency and the director approved the transfer to the relevant department for handling. However, Cao Mingwu, the drafting officer, believed that the full text stated that 'hereafter, complaints against officials that do not follow the prescribed procedures will not be accepted,' which should be made known to the public. Therefore, he added the phrase 'announce to the public' in addition to the transfer. However, he failed to handle the section concerning the Huangmei County Party Headquarters separately. This was his mistake and there was no other intention. The department also sent the government the department's files for review. It was found that the director of the department did not approve the order to issue a notice to the subordinate agencies. The drafting officer's handling was incorrect and highly inappropriate. The department was instructed to order the Public Security Bureau and other agencies to revoke the second notice. This is the process by which the government handled the matter after discovering the incident. Now, in accordance with your letter, in addition to ordering the Civil Affairs Department to withdraw Training Order No. 2725 and revoke all notices posted by its affiliated agencies, the government must also state that since the government was reorganized, it has received the spirit of cooperation between your association and the party, and has worked together with all its heart. The colleagues of the government deeply admire this. Director Meng has served under the party for many years and has always worked harmoniously with party agencies. He has no intention of insulting or attacking the party. This incident occurred due to an error by the drafting officer. Not only does the director deeply blame himself, but the government also deeply regrets it. In addition to the department already punishing the person responsible, we hereby reply for your information." (17th)

Shandong's Provincial Telephone Network Expected to Be Completed by the End of This Year; Active Reorganization of Provincial and County Telephones

Jinan Correspondence: The provincial telephone network is one of the major construction projects in the province in recent years. Of the province's 108 counties, 102 have telephone branch offices, with a total of 11,966 li of telephone lines. Only Tancheng in southern Shandong, and Rongcheng, Wendeng, Muping in eastern Shandong, and Shidao Town in the Weihai area have not yet been completed. The remaining areas are fully equipped. The Department of Construction is now actively constructing the unfinished areas, aiming to complete the great task of the provincial telephone network by the end of this year. After the turn of the year, the entire province will be able to communicate fully, in all directions. This will not only allow government orders to be communicated to the entire province instantly, but also greatly facilitate the transmission of news for merchants and the public. The provincial and county long-distance telephones are also being actively improved. The provincial telephones are the main lines of the Jinan-Yi, Jinan-Cao, Jinan-Dong, Jinan-Wu, and Jinan-Lai districts, all with Jinan as their hub. However, due to the large number of lines within the city, there are often disturbances. Starting today, the reorganization of various lines in Jinan City will begin to ensure clear voice transmission. All 108 counties have established county-owned telephones. County-owned lines and provincial-owned lines can be connected to each other for communication. However, county-owned lines are mostly single lines, while provincial-owned lines are mostly double lines. However, due to the burden of telephones in various counties, their effectiveness is also equivalent to single lines. Previously, the Department of Construction convened a meeting of telephone bureau chiefs, who resolved to request the Department of Construction to instruct all counties to change to double lines. They are currently being converted and will soon be completely improved. (17th)

Qingpu

Old Woman Commits Suicide After Being Humiliated

Xu Zhu, a resident of Zhujiajiao Town, Second District of this county, was known for her shrewish nature. Twenty years ago, her husband, Xu Kangmin, committed suicide by swallowing opium smoke out of anger at Zhu's improper behavior. On the 20th of last month, her aunt, Xi, suddenly secretly swallowed the water Zhu used to wash her hair and face with, and then committed suicide. It was widely rumored that Zhu had recently demanded a title deed from her aunt to provide her lover, Gu, as collateral for a loan, but her request was not granted, and she harbored deep resentment. Moreover, on the night of the twelfth, Gu was in Zhu's room when he was caught by her aunt, which led to an argument. Zhu slapped Xi's face. Xi, who was old and humiliated, committed this tragedy. The Xu clan was outraged and Zhu fled immediately. It is said that the case has been filed with the county government and is scheduled to be heard on the 23rd of this month.

Wuxi

Special Investigator from the Baoye Commission Arrives in Wuxi

Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry, in order to develop the national industry and rescue the economic panic, divided the country into six industrial survey areas. Each area was assigned a director and a number of investigators were appointed to be responsible for investigating the industrial conditions in the area. Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces were divided into one area, and Mei Songnan was appointed as the director of the investigation. After being appointed, Mei immediately began to carry out the investigation and decided that the survey locations in Jiangsu Province would be 12 counties, including Shanghai, Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Wuxian, Jiangdu, Wujin, Jiangyin, Huaiyin, Nantong, Changshu, Tongshan, and Wuxi. The scope of the investigation was divided into categories such as agriculture, industry, commerce, fisheries and animal husbandry, minerals, economic cooperatives, labor schools, labor-management disputes, special industries, and agricultural products. The size of the region, the length of the facts, and the differences in nature were used to appropriately classify and conduct precise surveys. The reports were submitted in stages at any time, and the investigation forms were compiled and reviewed. There were as many as 63 types. The deadline was June 1934. Mei came to Wuxi the day before yesterday and stayed at the Railway Hotel. He immediately started the investigation. The county government of this county sent staff to guide and assist him. So far, only one-third of the entire planned work has been investigated. The most difficult thing to investigate is that the persons in charge of the factories are mostly unwilling to report the actual situation in detail, so it is difficult to obtain the truth. However, Wuxi is a prosperous area with many factories, and there are more labor-management disputes than in other counties. Recently, the Huisheng Silk Factory went bankrupt due to debts, and the factory owner absconded with the money. Workers at the Ganshen Silk Factory also launched a strike due to issues such as work treatment. All of this exposes the economic panic. The failure to take into account the lives and education of workers is the most noteworthy point in the industrial survey.

Special Commissioner's Office Thoroughly Investigates Murder Case

Gong Yuezhou, the head of Xia Yu Township in the Fourth District, and villagers Wu A'er and Feng Baogen, etc., opened a gambling den in the Bai Shou Temple in Daishang Village of the township on the 12th of last month. Liu Chunlan, the head of the Ninth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, sent police officers to arrest the gamblers Wu Ating and Ma Xuxing, etc., totaling seven people. During the chaos, Gu Zongxiang and Wu Genshou drowned after falling into the river. The county court prosecutor then went to examine the bodies and released the gamblers and the police officers involved on bail. The villagers then accused the chief of the branch bureau, Liu Chunlan, of multiple offenses and filed a complaint with the provincial government. The Department of Civil Affairs ordered the county to dismiss Liu first and wait for investigation. Yesterday, Hou Ticheng, an investigator from the Second District Commissioner's Office, came to Wuxi to thoroughly investigate the case. He first went to the scene of the incident to investigate, and then went to the County Court, County Government, and Public Security Bureau to investigate. He returned to Changzhou the same night to report back.

Changshu

Large Quantity of Opium Seized at Port

At 1:00 PM on the 19th, the Suchang morning shift Jixing Wheel arrived in Changshu. When the wheel was alongside the shore, a passenger from another province stood at the bow of the ship, carrying a small leather suitcase, intending to be the first to disembark. Unexpectedly, he was seen by Song Peigen, a petitioner police officer from the Wheel Bureau. Recently, after the robbery of the wheel during the day, the inspection of suspicious persons was extremely strict. The passenger saw the police officer paying attention and returned to the cabin, disembarking from the stern of the ship and heading straight to the small alley of Yizhuang Lane. The police officer chased after him, wanting to check his suitcase. The man deliberately broke the key, claiming that it could not be opened. The police officer became more suspicious and asked him to go to the Public Security Sub-station. The two men then began to conflict. Fortunately, another police officer arrived to help arrest him. Under the supervision of Inspector Song and others, the lock was opened and it was found to contain opium. The packages were engraved with the Ge Ganji brand, weighing a total of 276 taels, including 14 taels of red earth and one opium cake, weighing one catty and four taels. When questioned, the man gave his name as Cheng Xueyi, 32 years old, from Hefei, Anhui. He said that the box was entrusted to him by a friend and he did not know what was inside. However, the Public Security Bureau's investigation revealed that the opium was entrusted to him by Xiaojiangdong, a well-known opium trafficker in Suzhou, to be transported to Changshu and delivered to Xushi Town. The Public Security Sub-station believed that the case was serious and immediately sent the suspect and witnesses to the General Bureau for further investigation and legal processing.

Jiangyin

Jimei Pawnshop Expected to Reopen

The Jimei Pawnshop on West Street in this county, which was opened by Sheng Jisun, was about to be closed down by Sheng last year. Through the maintenance of local figures such as Zhu Danqing, the Sheng's Yuzhai Charity Association repeatedly discussed and agreed to join as a shareholder. Zhu Danqing and others raised another 100,000 yuan of capital, which has now been fully raised. On the 18th, a fundraising committee was convened at Yiyuan, and it was decided to raise another 50,000 yuan, pay Sheng 10,000 yuan in foreign currency, and clear the payment by the end of December. It is also a gospel for the future of the people's economy.

Jiaxing

Land Survey Implemented in the Urban Area

The Jiaxing County Government, under orders to reorganize the land and carry out a survey, began root mapping in the urban area around August of this year, and has achieved considerable results. It is now urgent to continue the household land mapping in order to achieve success. A survey team has been established and dispatched to carry out the work in the urban area. Landowners located in the urban area must fill in each item in detail on the household land survey form issued by the survey office. When the surveyors measure the land, they will hand in the survey form for review and personally lead the way to indicate the boundaries in order to emphasize land administration.

Gaoyou

Chen Dingyao and His Brother Tragically Murdered

Chen Dingyao and his younger brother Chen Si, from Haizhou, had served in the military for many years in the past. After leaving the military, they moved to Fanlu Township, Second District of Baoying, and purchased farmland, which has been many years. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 15th, sixteen thugs suddenly came and drew out sharp blades as they entered the house, hacking at Chen Dingyao and his brother Chen Si. The heads of the Chen brothers were split open, and they fell to the ground and died on the spot. The scene was extremely tragic. The thugs, seeing that their goal had been achieved, fled immediately. The Chen family has reported the case to the Baoying County Government, requesting an investigation, autopsy, and strict arrest and punishment of the murderers.

Hangzhou

Zhejiang Security Office Executes Bandit

The Zhejiang Provincial Security Office, based on the submission of a bandit named Chen Qiwang by the FenShui County Government, ordered an interrogation and confirmed that the bandit had conspired with Zhou Li, Mao Cun, and seven others in the home of Wang Yang in Si Ling Township, FenShui County, to jointly rob and kidnap Yang Qi, Ye Da Zhu, demanding a ransom of 1,000 yuan. They later released Ye after receiving 150 yuan. The bandit shared the stolen money and hid in the home of Ye Pinnai in Danxia Wu, where he was arrested by the security regiment. The victim testified that he was definitely a robber. Chen also confessed to his crimes. He was sentenced to death and executed by shooting outside Qingbo Gate at 8:00 AM yesterday (19th) after verifying his identity.

Huzhou

Ferocious Woman Buries Maid Alive

In Jingwan, Meixi Town, Huzhou, there is a farmer named Li Xiantong, from Henan. Recently, due to livelihood difficulties, he sold his biological daughter, Zai Mao, to Wang Laoqi, a villager near Jingwan, as a maid last year. At that time, Zai Mao was only seven years old. However, Wang Laoqi was born cruel and often abused Zai Mao, resulting in her body being covered with scars. Li Xiantong had repeatedly heard that his daughter was suffering, but due to circumstances, he could only sigh. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 13th of this month, Wang Laoqi inhumanly carried Zai Mao to Heshangdun near Jingwan and buried her alive. When her body was half-buried, Zai Mao cried and wept in pain, begging pitifully. The person digging the burial discovered her conscience and stopped working. Li Xiantong, the girl's father, had heard the news and rushed to the scene. He took Zai Mao back, and she was able to live again. However, Zai Mao's body was covered with scars and she was seriously ill. It is said that Li plans to sue the court and arrest Wang to face the law.

Pinghu

Newspaper Editor Arrested for Framing

A local tabloid called "Social Daily" is run by Yao Shuizhang, the son of Yao Baoxing, a local constable. Since its publication, it has repeatedly been involved in lawsuits. Yesterday, Yao colluded with two Hunanese who had previously worked in the county government, and local retired police officers, posing as members of the anti-opium agency, to search Fuzhen Temple outside the North Gate for opium. When they searched the abbot's bedroom, Yao took out a paper package from his pocket, threw it on the bed, and said, "What is this if not opium?" Unexpectedly, the monks and laymen who were accompanying the inspection caught a glimpse and shouted that Yao was framing them. Yao immediately fled. This greatly angered the public, and many people gathered to arrest the two retired policemen. The rest scattered in the confusion. Yao Shuizhang returned to the city and reported to the Public Security Bureau, saying that their subordinates were extorting money outside the North Gate. He also went to the county government and reported to a certain official that the Public Security Bureau had instructed its subordinates to falsely accuse honest people in an attempt to shirk responsibility. After a while, the two offenders were brought in, and it was learned that Yao was the mastermind. The Public Security Bureau used an unexpected means to send police officers to his home in the middle of the night and arrest Yao. It was heard this afternoon that Yao and his accomplices would be sent to the county for thorough investigation.

Water Police Disturb Theater

Last night, as the Xinmin Theater in Beisi Lane was about to open, more than twenty water police officers suddenly rushed in and seized Xu Liansheng, an employee, and beat him in a circle. The theater was thrown into chaos, and bystanders were afraid of their ferocity and dared not intervene. They then dragged him out of the theater, punching, kicking, and stamping on him until he was covered in scars and blood. Then, they released him, formed a line, and left. The theater employees were confused. When they questioned Xu, he said that there was no animosity. However, yesterday, a deputy commander of the team came to watch the play, accompanied by a woman. He assumed that the deputy commander could enter without a ticket, but accompanying guests were required to pay. Therefore, he asked them to pay for the ticket. The deputy commander glared at him and ignored him. He was reluctant to argue with him. He had no other connection with them. The theater believes that the theater is a business for the people, and it should not be allowed for government officials to trample on it at will. They have prepared a telegram to complain to the province, and will not stop until the perpetrators are punished.

Xiaoshan

Collision of Sailing Boats Drowns Boatman

On the 18th at noon at Dongjiangzui, Qiantang River, Xiaoshan, a small pig boat coming from upstream and a firewood boat collided due to unfavorable winds and sails, resulting in a dispute. Ah Wei, the boatman of the small pig boat, knocked a crew member of the firewood boat into the river and drowned him. The crew members of the firewood boat gathered more than ten companions and threw all the small pigs into the river, totaling thirty-seven, most of which drowned. At that time, both parties went ashore at Wenyen and filed a lawsuit with the County Court.

Large Number of Jiangxi Refugees Disturb Peace

A large number of Jiangxi refugees arrived in Jiudun Anchang, Dongxiang, on the night of the 18th and disturbed the peace of every household. The Xu family in Jiudun was forced to give silver dollars by the refugees, resulting in the destruction of tables and chairs. On the 19th, they went to Yifeng and caused a great disturbance. The Xiang Office secretly reported to the Anchang Police Station, which sent police to suppress them and they were able to leave the area.

Shangyu

Expected Opening of the Haoshan-Shanshutang Section of the Road

The section from Haoba Town in the western part of this county to Shanshutang in Sheng County is approximately eighty li long and is an important route connecting the counties of Shaoxing, Xiaoshan, Yu, Sheng, and XinFeng. It is important for transportation and military purposes. The construction was started last winter by the Shaoxing-Sheng Motor Company and has been underway for one year.
