Education News from Other Cities

Guo Youshou Inspects Shandong Province's Education and Criticizes It

(Jinan Correspondence) Shandong education was completely destroyed by Zhang Zongchang. It was only after the success of the Northern Expedition that the work of reorganization began. Over the years, there has been considerable progress. The Ministry of Education specially appointed Guo Youshou to come to Shandong for inspection. The Department of Education sent the second section chief Lai Zhizhong to accompany him to various places in southern, northern, and eastern Shandong. After more than a month of detailed inspection, he finally arrived in Qingdao and returned to Jinan today (the 18th). After returning from studying abroad, Guo was sent by the Ministry of Education to countries such as Soviet Russia and Denmark for inspection. He has extensive knowledge. His observations and criticisms of the education in this province after a long period of inspection are very important. The reporter specially visited him today to ask about everything. The following is a record of what Mr. Guo said.

▲ General Criticism: Guo said: "I have been sent by the Ministry to inspect education in Shandong for more than a month. The places I have visited include Jinan City, Tai'an, Qufu, Yanzhou, Jining, Qihe, Pingyuan, Dexian, Zhangqiu, Zouping, Changshan, Qingzhou, Weixian, Huangxian, Yantai, Qingdao, etc. The schools I have inspected include provincial normal schools, middle schools, vocational schools, local educational administrative organs, county middle schools, elementary schools, normal training schools, vocational supplementary schools, mass education centers, and civilian schools. In general, the zoning plan for normal schools is very good. Regarding provincial normal schools, I inspected the First Normal School, the First Women's Normal School, the Second Normal School, the Fourth Normal School, and the Fourth and Fifth Rural Normal Schools, etc. I inspected high schools, the First Middle School, the First Women's Middle School, the Third Middle School, the Seventh Middle School, the Twelfth Middle School, the Tenth Middle School, and the Eighth Middle School, etc. I inspected private middle schools, including Dezhou Bowei, Yantai Yiwen, Zhifu, Jining Sino-Western, Weixian Guangwen, and Tai'an Cuiying and Yuying. I inspected provincial vocational schools, including the First, Second, and Third Vocational Schools, etc. The Department of Education has predetermined plans for the above three types of schools: normal schools, middle schools, and vocational schools. The locations of the schools are also fairly appropriate and can serve as centers. The principals of the schools are working very hard within the possible scope, and the students are also very diligent and thrifty.

▲ Normal Education: At the Provincial Fourth Rural Normal School, the principal and faculty lead the students in labor, jointly transporting bricks and tiles for construction, which is quite a new phenomenon. Their civilian schools, short-term elementary schools, etc., have all been established. For example, the farm raises chickens, ducks, and cattle, and also keeps bees, preparing to use it as a pilot area for the mass education center. The school has experiments for transforming the countryside (there are textbooks on transforming rural teaching materials). All students and faculty are working in one direction, and it is hoped that other rural normal schools will also strive to go to the countryside. As for county rural normal schools, Qihe is the best. With very little funding, they live in the Confucian Temple, and the houses are also very dilapidated. After rectification, they have made considerable progress, and the teachers and students are very excited. All county-level normal training schools are limited by financial and human resources and have not been able to fully develop.

▲ Vocational Mechanical: The First, Second, and Third Vocational Schools that were inspected all have dyeing and weaving as a common subject. The First Vocational School has machinery as its special feature. Chemistry is not very complete in each school. The First and Third Vocational Schools are expected to develop. The principals of the three schools have studied industry and can realistically seek a way out for the students within their scope, so that the students have the skills to make a living after graduation. However, it is a pity that they cannot be fully developed due to limited funding. It is hoped that dyeing, weaving, leather making, and machinery can be expanded for students to practice. As for vocational supplementary education, it is often nominal.

▲ Secondary Education: The provincial middle schools are working hard to prepare students for further education and are strictly training them. Private middle schools, Bowei, divide students into groups for English, Chinese, and arithmetic training, so that those with talent can make great progress, and those with slightly lower levels can also reach the minimum curriculum standards. There are plans for labor education. Students in the school can repair their own bicycles, which is one example. Zhifu Middle School has impressive school buildings and facilities. Among the county middle schools, Huangxian County Middle School is quite tidy. Principal Zhao Zhurong is working hard to raise funds to expand the facilities.

▲ Compulsory Education: Among the counties inspected for compulsory education, Qihe's method is the most comprehensive, and the rural elementary schools are also very tidy. Two-thirds of the school-age children in the county have the opportunity to study. Qi Fengtu, the fifth section chief of the county, continued the plan of the former section chief Wang Xuxing. The designated school districts are very well arranged. Generally, there is an elementary school every two li. The source of funding is apportioned according to the area of land. The county is not a wealthy area, but it has been able to achieve its current achievements, which is very pleasing. Although this method of apportioning money by the mu is very good, it is a pity that it cannot be used as an example for other counties due to the limitations of the central laws. There are the most civilian schools in Tai'an, reaching more than 60 schools in the county. As for short-term compulsory education, its promotion is not yet widespread.

Inspection Feelings: The feeling of this inspection is that Shandong education is still stable and generally on the right track. It is not easy to have the current achievements. The education section chiefs and supervisors of each county have no separation from the department. However, the common problem of provincial secondary schools is that 80% of the funding is used for salaries, and very little funding is used for other office purchases. There is no funding for adding specimens, instruments, and books. Labor education, woodworking, and metalworking are completely lacking. The teacher clock rate is also not very suitable for the Department regulations. This should be corrected in the afternoon budget. The item of books, instruments, and specimens must account for 20% of the total funding, and the number of staff and workers should be reduced as much as possible. Regarding elementary schools, the problems in each county are inconsistent. There are those with sufficient funding but lack of students, and those with insufficient funding but many students. The lack of teachers is felt in the countryside because the salaries of rural schools are very low, so normal school students are unwilling to go to the countryside. The salaries of rural teachers are as low as three and a half yuan a month. The education bureaus also do not audit the budgets of the schools, which should be strictly regulated. The Department of Education should also increase direct supervision. The curriculum allocation and teaching methods of the complex elementary schools should be improved. Rural women's education is too underdeveloped, and the holidays are irregular. Measures should be taken to make up for the lessons. In the future, the Department of Education should impose restrictions and allocate the service period of normal school graduates to serve in the countryside. The education in Lubei is better because it is more prosperous. For the promotion of compulsory education, each county should be strict and expand it in the shortest possible time. The people of Huangxian are wealthy and mostly engaged in business in the Northeast, so the school should specially let the students understand the situation in the Northeast. The local education funding in the county is too small and mostly relies on private donations. The equipment of the First Elementary School in the Third District of the county is the most complete. The library in the school has more than 30,000 books. All instruments can also be used by the faculty for research. Among the twelve faculty members in the school, seven or eight are voluntary. The school's eleven classes of students only have a funding of more than a thousand yuan. The human body models made by the students are extremely exquisite. The school relies entirely on the operation of the school trustee Zhang Tiqing, which is commendable. This school is rare in the country, and the government should reward it. There are eleven private middle schools in Yantai that have not been registered, and 43 elementary schools, with only six registered. The area is a seaport commercial port with abundant small produce and many group properties, all important. The government should pay special attention.

▲ Inspection Purpose: This mission has two main purposes: (1) Inspect vocational education. According to the regulations of the Ministry of Education, the funding for secondary vocational schools should not be less than 35% of the funding for secondary schools, ordinary middle schools should not be more than 40%, and normal schools should not be less than 20%. Currently, the funding for middle schools in Shandong has exceeded 43%, while the funding for vocational schools only accounts for 9%. The courses in each vocational school are similar, with only three subjects: dyeing, weaving, chemistry, and machinery. The number of vocational schools and subjects should also be increased as needed locally. In Yantai, there should be fruit and horticulture; in Boshan, there should be porcelain and glass; in Weixian, there should be dyeing, weaving, and machinery; and in Linqing, there should be agriculture, all of which should be established to meet the standards of the Ministry. Short-term vocational training should be provided in various fields, such as farming, industry, and weaving, such as dyeing and weaving, shop assistants, hairdressers, waiters, and ironworkers, and should be given short-term scientific training. There are too many county middle schools in each place, and they should be converted into vocational schools, because middle schools are too empty and can only prepare for further education. Society must make everyone value vocational education. Like the schools in Soviet Russia, they are all industrialized. The local funding in each county should give priority to the development of compulsory education, not the development of middle schools. Shandong's normal education is well-developed, and the Department of Education should have an overall statistic. The Department of Education should also thoroughly investigate and register the talents inside and outside the province for employment. There are too many classes in middle schools, and the number of students is uncertain, which does not meet the principles of middle schools. (2) Independent educational funding. The second purpose is to strive for independent, guaranteed, and auditable educational funding in each province and city. Shandong's local educational funding is already independent, so there is no difficulty. The provincial educational funding has also increased since Chairman Han (Fu Ju) came to Shandong, so there seems to be no need to be independent immediately. The auditing of the Department of Education in this province has also achieved the greatest success. In summary, the impressions gained from the inspection in Shandong for these two major purposes are very satisfactory. The number of schools has increased greatly, and the promotion of mass education has also achieved good results. The work of the Provincial Mass Education Center is intense and can gain the welcome of the masses. If more rural teachers can become central leaders in the countryside, it will lay the foundation for the restoration of the countryside. The colleagues in the Department of Education are very serious about conducting the joint examinations, and the parents of all students approve.

▲ Establish an Education Museum: It is hoped that Shandong will establish an education museum in the future, with instruments, health specimens, etc., for research, and it is hoped that all educational institutions and schools can be completely interconnected and integrated, and can often meet in different places to learn from each other, so that each school can adopt the local teaching materials, so as to know the local situation. Labor education should also be implemented based on what is available locally, etc.

Anhui Education Department Increases the Authority of Supervisors

(Anqing Correspondence) The deterioration of education in Anhui Province is undeniable. In previous years, after the start of each semester, the Education Department would dispatch supervisors to inspect various districts. However, the results were merely a perfunctory official report that was vague and did not address the specific management of each school, or whether the principals and teachers were competent. This led to a culture of following routines and being perfunctory. Now, the Education Department Director Yang Lian, in order to promote education, has divided the province's fifty-seven counties into five inspection zones and dispatched the department's supervisors to each zone. The zones are: (1) First Zone, Huaining and thirteen other counties, Ye Minghui; (2) Second Zone, Wuhu and twelve other counties, Wei Congxu; (3) Third Zone, Qingyang and eleven other counties, Zhang Shaolie; (4) Fourth Zone, Chuzhou and eleven other counties, Chen Mingxin; (5) Fifth Zone, Su County and ten other counties, Zhou Yuanji. Public and private primary and secondary schools and social education institutions in the provincial capital will be inspected jointly or in groups by the supervisors. The four counties of Liu'an, Huoqiu, Baoshan, and Lihuang have suffered from banditry and will be reorganized by specially assigned officials. After being appointed, these officials have already set off on their respective journeys. It is said that the Education Department has granted these supervisors considerable real power for this inspection. If the education bureau chiefs, principals, and teachers in each county are found to be competent, they will be immediately recommended to the department for commendation; otherwise, they will be immediately replaced. We do not know whether the future of education in Anhui Province will be completely changed by this departure from the old ways.

New Building of National Central University Library Completed

(Nanjing, 20th, Central News Agency) The new building of the National Central University Library was completed on the 20th. The construction and equipment cost a total of 200,000 yuan. The reading room and research rooms can accommodate 900 people, making it the largest library in the capital. It will be open in one month.

Chinese Education Society Decides to Hold First Annual Meeting in Beijing

▲ Build New Club House and Run Experimental School

▲ Request the Academia Sinica to Establish an Education Research Institute

The Chinese Education Society held its third committee meeting yesterday (the 19th) starting at 9:00 AM at the YMCA in Ba Xian Qiao. At 6:00 PM, the Zhonghua Book Company hosted a banquet at the same location. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

Attending Committee Members: Yesterday's attending committee members included Tao Zhihxing, Zhuang Posexuan, Zheng Xigu, Shao Shuangqiu, Ou Yuanhuai, Chang Daozhi, Yang Lianggong, Xu Keshi, Liu Tingfang, Zheng Xiaocang, and more than ten others. Chairman was Liu Tingfang, and the recorder was Shao Shuangqiu.

Reports: (1) Xu Keshi reported on the Ministry of Education's order to issue survey forms and the status of income and expenditure; (2) Zheng Xigu reported on the transfer of donations from members when Chen Kemei handed over the preparatory committee in Fuzhou, the takeover of the Central Education Research Institute, and the Sino-French Boxer Indemnity subsidy; (3) Zheng Xiaocang reported on the editing of the special issue on the transformation of Chinese education; (4) Tao Zhihxing reported on the compilation of educational books and newspapers; (5) Zheng Xigu reported on the experimental survey plan.

Important Resolutions: (1) He Baicheng resigned from the committee for preparing the education library due to illness. It was resolved to express sympathy for his illness in the name of the association and to persuade him to stay; (2) It was resolved to add Tao Zhihxing as a preparatory committee member for preparing the association's education library; (3) It was resolved to appoint Xu Keshi, Yang Lianggong, Zheng Xigu, and Tao Zhihxing as preparatory committee members responsible for planning the construction of the clubhouse and the operation of the experimental school; (4) Chang Daozhi resigned from the standing director and resident director because he changed his job to a professor at Beijing Normal University. It was resolved to persuade him to stay and grant him leave, with Yang Lianggong acting on his behalf; (5) It was resolved to determine the location and date of the first annual meeting. It was resolved to consult with the Kaifeng committee and set it for January 26th and 27th of the 23rd year in Nanjing, and the preparatory matters were entrusted to the Nanjing branch; (6) Zheng Xiaocang's request for retroactive recognition of the contract signed with the Zhonghua Book Company for the printing of the special issue on the transformation of Chinese education was approved; (7) The request to the Ministry of Education for a subsidy for the experimental survey was resolved to be handled by the original committee; (8) Tao Zhihxing resigned from the committee for the compilation of educational book and newspaper abstracts, which was approved, and He Shuangqiu and Zhuang Zexuan were appointed as committee members; (9) The proposal to request the Academia Sinica to establish an education research institute was resolved to be directly sent to the Academia Sinica requesting its prompt establishment; (10) The proposal to request the China Education and Culture Foundation Board of Directors to subsidize education research was resolved to have the standing directors draft a plan and submit it to the next council for discussion on the method; (11) New members were approved for membership. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM. That evening, the Zhonghua Book Company hosted a banquet for the committee members at the same location, during which there was a detailed discussion on publishing matters.

Regulations for Private Schools Revised

The Municipal Education Bureau Instructed to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an instruction to the city's private schools yesterday, stating that it had received Instruction No. 10848 from the Ministry of Education, which stated that the regulations for private schools promulgated by the Ministry in August of the 18th year had been revised. A copy of the revised regulations for private schools was enclosed. The instruction ordered compliance. Upon receiving this, the bureau stated that the procedure for registering cases under the revised regulations for private schools has been simplified compared to before. However, new private schools must comply with the provisions of paragraph 1 of Article 26, and schools must not rush to enroll students without the approval of the competent education administrative authority. In the future, if new schools are to be established, preparations must be made early and reported for approval. After approval by the Bureau or the Ministry of Education, enrollment can be advertised. The other articles have also been slightly revised. All private schools under its jurisdiction are instructed to comply with the regulations.

Educational Film Association Screens Educational Films in Rural Pudong Yesterday

▲ Three Thousand Farmers from Four Villages Participate

▲ Boy Scouts and Security Corps Maintain Order

▲ Fourth Round of School Screenings Begins

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Educational Film Association has been screening educational films in schools throughout the city for nearly two months. The films shown have been carefully selected and arranged, so that the content is both educational and entertaining, and they have been well received by students in various schools. Yesterday, the association went to the rural areas of Pudong to show films, reaching deep into the civilian population. The fourth round of school screenings has also begun, and details are recorded as follows:

Yesterday afternoon, during the dedication ceremony of the new school building at Tangpan Municipal Primary School in Tangqiao Town, Pudong, the school sent a letter to the association requesting a special screening. Approximately 3,000 people, including students from the school and farmers from the surrounding villages, attended. Boy Scouts and security corps were present to maintain order. It was the only educational gathering of its kind in Pudong recently. The screening was completed at 9:00 PM, and the audience expressed deep satisfaction.

Since the beginning of this month, the association has begun the third round of educational films in various schools in the city, and has been showing films to about a dozen schools every day for the past two weeks. The number of students attending often reaches more than 5,000, and they all praise the films as more interesting reading material than textbooks. Currently, the work of producing subtitles and compiling explanatory brochures for the fourth round of educational films has been completed, and screenings in various schools have begun.

Educational Seminar Discusses Middle School Chinese Teaching Methods

▲ Yesterday's Third Gathering

▲ Chen Zhuzun and Others Give Lectures

The newly initiated educational seminar in the Shanghai education community held its third gathering at 3:00 PM on the 19th of this month at Guanshengyuan on Nanjing Road. Chinese teachers from 29 schools including Provincial Shanghai Middle School, Municipal Wuben, Minli, Minli Women's Middle School, Yuqing Middle School, Dazhong Middle School, Fudan Experimental Middle School, Aiqun Women's Middle School, Junyi Middle School, Youth Middle School, Xuhui Middle School, Xinhuan Vocational Middle School, Dagong Vocational Middle School, Huiqun Women's Middle School, Huadong Women's Middle School, and Taihu Junior Middle School, as well as Hong Weifa, Liu Xunmu, Huang Zuyi, He Xianqi, Chen Tianhong, Jin Dingyi, Tu Shaokai, Zhao Jingshen, Fan Shuhan, Zhang Zhonghuan, Li Qixiu, Jiang Jingyu, Ma Jiazhen, Tao Jianhua, and Xu Wancheng, more than 40 people in total, attended. First, the initiator Xu Wancheng delivered a speech, stating that today we are gathered here, all of us are middle school Chinese teachers, and there are many senior veterans in attendance. He hoped that everyone would express their opinions on middle school Chinese teaching methods in order to improve them. Then, Chen Zhuzun, chairman of the Chinese Department of Jiaotong University, gave a lecture, first stating his experiences as a Chinese professor in middle school, and also stating that the selection of Chinese teaching materials must be simple, and more emphasis should be placed on applied writing. Next, Yan Junxuan of Aiqun Women's Middle School said that middle school Chinese teaching must focus on grammar and composition, so that students' writing can be fluent. Subsequently, Ma Chong of Yuqing Middle School, Hong Weifa of Shanghai Middle School, Tu Shaokai of Minli Middle School, and Zhang Zhonghuan of Xinhuan Vocational Middle School successively expressed their opinions, omitting the length of their speeches. At the end, the Beixin Book Company presented Mixed Mandarin and Middle School Anthologies, requesting concrete criticism. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

Ministry of Education and General Training Department Cooperation Plan for Physical Education Colleges Canceled

丨Decided to Establish Separately丨

▲ Ministry of Education 丨 National College of Physical Education

▲ Training Department 丨 Military Physical Education College

(Nanjing, 20th) The Ministry of Education and the General Training Department's joint venture to run physical education colleges was discussed by Zhang Jiong, Director of the Social Affairs Department of the Ministry of Education, and the General Training Department. Because one side focuses on military physical education and the other focuses on public and school physical education, it was decided to run two schools separately. The Ministry of Education is named the National College of Physical Education, and the Training Department is named the Military Physical Education College. Both parties will still cooperate on the recruitment of teachers and the standards to be met. The Ministry of Education's preparation for the establishment of the college is underway.

Chongde Surprises Everyone, Victory Over Liangjiang Not Easy

丨Result 32 to 19丨

Southeast vs. Jinan Tonight

The Chongde Women's Basketball Team surprised everyone last night, playing against Liangjiang. The score was tied at 16 to 16 in the second half. At the end of the third quarter, Liangjiang led by only one point, with the score at 20 to 19. But in the last eight minutes, Chongde was defeated, and the final result was 32 to 19. Chongde's defense was tight, leaving the opponent with no gaps to exploit. The forwards were lively and accurate in their shots. Although they were small and weak, their defeat was still honorable. There were originally two women's basketball games scheduled for last night, but two teams were late by fifteen minutes, and the referee announced their disqualification. Guanghua won without a fight.

Remotely Occupied the Upper Hand

After the start of the game, Chongde gave Liangjiang a fierce resistance, and the situation was very tense. He Miaoying and Wei Peixun missed several shots. After three minutes of stalemate, Chen Rongming and Chen Xuefang of Liangjiang each scored. Chongde returned a goal by He Miaoying. From then on, Liangjiang's brilliance gradually emerged, and Chen Rongming showed great power, scoring repeatedly. In the first quarter, Liangjiang took the lead with a score of 10 to 2.

Catching Up Quickly

Starting from the second quarter, the situation became very tense. The Chongde girls were not willing to be outdone, and they shook off their spirits and quickly caught up. Liangjiang's defense suddenly became difficult to defend, becoming a time of trouble. The two Misses Wei and He scored every shot they made. Liangjiang's forwards were trapped in tight defense and found it difficult to move. The balls they passed out were often intercepted by the opponent, and there were not many opportunities to shoot. This quarter ended 8 to 6, with Chongde taking the lead, but Liangjiang still led by 16 to 10 in the first half overall.

Score Equal

Starting in the second half, Chongde's spirit became even stronger, and Liangjiang's forwards had almost no chance to get the ball. Chongde's forwards were resourceful and handy. Wei Peixun was short and strong, He Miaoying was petite and exquisite, and Wang Fengqun provided effective support. Three consecutive goals were scored, resulting in a 16 to 16 tie. The Chongde girls were overjoyed. Liangjiang saw the opportunity and made a big move, immediately sending Yang Sen onto the court to save the situation. Two consecutive goals were scored, making the score 20 to 16. Chongde continued to work hard, adding three points. In the third quarter, Chongde was behind with a score of 19 to 20.

Declining Rapidly

Starting in the fourth quarter, Liangjiang made a final effort and returned to its full glory. Chongde's physical and mental strength was exhausted. Although they wanted to make a final struggle, their heart was willing, but their strength was insufficient. From then on, the score remained stalled, and they were unable to do anything. The Liangjiang girls took advantage of the situation and scored twelve consecutive points, winning the final victory with a score of 32 to 19.

Tonight's Order

Spring and Autumn

On Roundness and Squareness

— Anfu

Generally speaking, a shape without sharp corners is called round. The shape of an object that is upright is called square. Round is the opposite of square; square is the opposite of round. Even small children know these two opposing shapes.

Round and square are originally nouns describing states; however, there are also differences in their prominence and obscurity in their fate. The round thing, it can be said, is the best symbol of both ancient and modern times, especially the thoroughly modernized present. Generally speaking, when describing the temperament of ordinary people, those who can be accommodating are called well-rounded, and those who are harmonious are called harmonious. In Buddhism, those who are quick-witted and enlightened are called perfect and wonderful. Therefore, Guanyin Bodhisattva is also called the Great Master of Perfect Understanding. The sky is also called round spirit or round sugar, and the earth is also round. Beautiful women are called round. A full moon also represents perfect reunion. Even foreign coins, jiao coins, and copper plates are all round. True beauties and money are both round, and one must also think from a round perspective to gain reputation. What else do the myriad living beings in the world seek besides these three? Roundness is truly the only treasure in the world.

As for the square thing, it is not right. We only need to look at the common saying "square handle in a round mortise" to understand. Squareness is actually an inauspicious adjective, the most annoying, and also the most out of touch with the times. For example, dialects cannot be widely used (Fang Yan, not written by Yang Xiong). Magical arts cannot reach the height of elegance. A person who is upright is scolded as a dead Amu Lin. The statements of alchemists are absurd. And Fang Hui of the Song Dynasty was despised by people. Fang Xiaoru of the Ming Dynasty was killed, and ten generations of his family were exterminated. In short, squareness is an inauspicious thing.

Squareness is the most useless thing in the present. Roundness is a necessary tool for being a person. I can't help but shout for roundness and wish you longevity!

Coal Gas Poisoning

— Yongzi

Cholera has lost its empire, and red and white dysentery has also fallen from the throne. The autumn wind is blowing so strongly. Well, from now on, "coal gas poisoning" should be a wonderful embellishment in the daily social news.

The rich people cover themselves with silk quilts and wool blankets, and heat water radiators and electric heaters. They are warm and hygienic. The poor people wear tattered cotton jackets and cover themselves with old, tattered quilts. Damn it, they are frozen awake in the quilts before midnight. How can they endure until dawn? Okay, let's move the coal briquette stove for cooking to the front of the bed tomorrow! Add enough coal briquettes, and it'll be warm and comfortable. But, this comfort is not a big deal, but tomorrow there may be a danger of "deeply poisoned, incurable."

From this "coal gas poisoning" incident, we are reminded of many "coal gas poisoning" things in society.

When I was studying as a child, I was most afraid of serious teachers, especially during small and big exams, absolutely not allowing cheating or copying books. Therefore, serious teachers are often sacrificed by the trend, while mediocre teachers receive strong support. This situation is no different from sleeping next to a coal briquette stove.

After arguing with my wife two or three times, damn it, I'll go out and play with women. It's not like I can't get comfort other than my wife. But, uh, I spent a lot of money and only got a little bit of her affection. This is still considered good. If you're unlucky and encounter a honey trap and get a venereal disease, your reputation will be ruined. This is "deeply poisoned, incurable."

No money to spend, borrow money. No place to borrow at low interest, borrow usurious loans. The money is borrowed and spent comfortably, and I feel relieved. But before I can feel relieved, the creditor is already knocking on the door with a livid face. Unable to repay the principal and interest, I have no choice but to be grabbed by the creditor's chest, slapped with a big palm, and with tears and snot, regret that I should not have been indecisive, resulting in "coal gas poisoning."

Whether it is a large country or a small individual, seeking temporary pleasure while ignoring the possible dangers is inevitable to suffer from "coal gas poisoning." This is a lesson for standing in the world.

Needle

— Fu Hongyi

Don't regret yesterday, don't hope for tomorrow, but respect today. Don't resent the past, don't calculate the future, but grasp the present.

In a realistic society, if you want to find friends with pure hearts and faithful behavior, you can only run to the children's team.

The "No Urinating" sign is not effective, so "Offenders will be sent to the police" or "Urinators will be fined five yuan" are added under "No Urinating." But, in the end, it's still the same. Here, I have to learn from Lu Xun and say, "Understanding these things is understanding most of the Chinese people."

Punishment for Sleeping

— Xie Jiju

If Zai Yu sleeps during the day, it is certainly "rotten wood cannot be carved," but Confucius only lamented Zai Yu's unsuitability, and did not revoke his qualification to hear the Dao. Not revoking his qualification to hear the Dao is to want him to understand the Dao, know his mistakes, and perhaps also be able to change his ways and become a complete person because he knows where his mistakes are. This is not impossible.

Recently, a certain university gave student A "a demerit" for "dozing in class." At the same time, a student in the school's attached middle school was also sleeping in class, so the school authorities "considering his first offense," ingeniously gave the student the punishment of "not being allowed to take civics class" and posted it publicly for all to know.

It is also an undeniable fact that students in general have become too casual in class recently. Sleeping in class certainly has to be punished, and giving a demerit is not inappropriate in terms of educational principles, in the sense of punishing one to warn a hundred. But whether it is appropriate to not allow him to take civics class still needs to be considered. You need to know that civics is a science that teaches people about perfect personality, and is the theoretical course of school education. Students read civics to understand the rules of being a person, understand common malpractices and mistakes, and then eliminate them, and walk on the path to a perfect life. Because a student sleeps in class, he is not allowed to take civics class, in other words, he is not allowed to have the right to be a citizen. This punishment for sleeping really needs to be studied and criticized by educators!

A Story of Beards

— Canye

In ancient Eastern nations, there was a deep superstition that a man's beard was a symbol of glory, and when punishing someone, they would force him to shave off his beard and cut his hair short. But looking at ancient Assyrian sculptures, the images of the emperors are all with long beards fluttering in front of their chests, and their hair is always long, while the slaves serving on the left and right do not have a single beard, shaving their faces clean, and their hair is also shaved like monks. The distinction between noble and lowly is of course obvious at a glance.

The opinions of the Egyptians, however, were different from those of the Assyrians. They believed that beards and hair were dirty things and parasites that sucked blood from the human body, so they had to shave their heads and faces completely. Their servants were also forced to do the same and were not allowed to keep them long.

In ancient Greece and Rome, when fighting against enemies, their beards were often grabbed and they were defeated, suffering greatly. Therefore, they all cut off their beards and hair, leaving no hair. It is said that King Alexander the Great strictly ordered his soldiers to shave their beards for this reason.

According to ancient Roman customs, when men turned twenty-one, they had to shave off their beards and offer them before the idols in their homes. When they grew their beards again after this age, it meant that a family member had died.

Four Northeast Company Commanders

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 19: Desiring to be together, yet wanting to separate, in the same car, recalling past events, half crying, half laughing, leaning on the pillow, sick in late autumn

On the avenue northeast of Haidian, the departing troops were marching further and further away, and a large group of people who came to see them off stood by the roadside, all dazed. Ms. Jiang saw Guizhi pinching the corner of her long coat, silently, slowly rubbing it there. Although she was standing facing the northeast corner, her eyes were looking at the closest piece of ground. She was naturally thinking about something, but was she feeling better in her heart, or was she not feeling better in her heart? This could not be known. Ms. Jiang took a step closer, stood close to her, and asked, "Girl, what's wrong with you? Let's go back." Guizhi smiled at her mother inexplicably and said, "That's right, we should go back. What are we waiting for?" After saying that, she walked in front. So, Zhao Weng and Huang Manying followed her into the house. The most wonderful thing was that they did not walk back to their backyard, but also followed to the Yang family. Ms. Jiang walked in front, sighed, and said, "In the past, when I saw soldiers, I hated them in my heart. Now when I see soldiers, I just pity them. I feel that what I did in the past was really wrong. If I have a son, I won't..." When she got to this point, Guizhi turned her head and smiled, "The old master is here too. Please sit down." Ms. Jiang smiled, "Look, I'm really careless, the old master is here, and I didn't see him. Girl, go make some boiling water." Zhao Weng was also inexplicable, how he followed his in-law mother and walked to this place. Since he had already walked into the door, there was no way he could leave without saying anything. He could only smile and say, "Don't bother, I see that you are feeling a little uncomfortable, and this Miss Huang also has a kind of unspeakable suffering in her heart, so I came to talk to everyone to relieve the boredom." Ms. Jiang smiled, "Oh! Can our hearts be more uncomfortable than the old master's?" Zhao Weng sat down and smiled, "Everything is a habit. My family Zi Qiang has been leaving me for a long time since he became an adult. Now that he is not in front of me, I don't miss him so much. He is such a big son, he can't be held in my arms and raised." (245)

Short Story

Gambling

— Zhu Yanying

It was agreed to be eight rounds, and then four more rounds were added. After twelve rounds of mahjong, it was almost one-thirty in the morning.

Walking out of my friend's front door, the north wind hit my face, and a chill rose from my heart. Although there were two partners walking with me, it could not make my thoughts linger on the joy any longer.

I arrived home, and my sister opened the door. Another feeling ran deep into my heart, and tears unconsciously fell down.

Mother was sick; my sister's eyebrows were tightly furrowed, showing worry. I came out early in the morning and only returned at this moment.

"Were you gambling again?"

I had no courage to ask how Mother was feeling, but Mother said this as soon as she saw me step in the door. I know that Mother was not complaining to me, because Mother is too kind and has never used harsh words to me. However, when I heard it, it was like being stabbed by a sharp blade! Ah! I should think carefully, did I do something wrong? I had no words to answer!

"Take care of your body!"

Recently, I have been obsessed with gambling, and I always come back at twelve or one o'clock every night. Mother said to take care of my body, but have I ever thought about it myself?

I turned on the light in my bedroom. Hearing Mother's painful coughing in the next room, grief occupied my whole mind and body.

Thanks to the care of my clan uncle, I was able to find this position, and my monthly income is five times more than before in the factory. Therefore, it is enough to maintain the livelihood of the whole family, so that we will not often fall into the abyss of hardship again. However, I suddenly became addicted to gambling, not returning home for dinner two or three times a week, and going to my colleagues' homes to play for winnings. Mother and sister are waiting at home, and the weather has become severe. They endure the cold for me, and tomorrow morning they still have to get up before dawn to cook breakfast for me for the sake of my office work.

Mother has been suffering from a cough these past few days, and the cough syrup has been ineffective, and it seems to only be getting worse. How could I not see Mother's illness as more important than my own winnings, and still gamble late into the night? Mother's illness may even be caused by me.

Money won also has a day to be spent, let alone that I have been poor until now, and I don't necessarily lack these few dollars I won. If I don't care about Mother's pain and indulge my own selfish desires, even if I can change from utter poverty to great wealth from today to tomorrow, how will I comfort my elderly Mother?

Lying in bed, the thoughts in my mind were like ten thousand horses galloping back and forth. I hated myself to the extreme!

My elderly Mother has endured hardship and suffered. Since Father died ten years ago, her teeth have fallen out one by one, and her white hair has gradually increased, but she doesn't feel sad or worried at all, but just labors with a smile, diligently raising her son! Me. What is the root cause of Mother's joy? I am very clear in my chest, but am I walking towards the goal that Mother expects, making Mother even more joyful? Alas! The truth is the opposite. Even if I kneel down and cry to Mother in repentance, there is no room for forgiveness!

The result of gambling is that I always lose. Three yuan, five yuan, the family's living expenses are captured by other people's cunning after each unsuccessful round of dominoes. On the one hand, I try my best to tell Mother and sister to be frugal, and that we should save a certain amount of money each month; and Mother and sister are really able to do as I say. I don't eat lunch at home, and they only cook porridge, swallowing it with a fried dough stick. And what about myself? Heavens! I am recklessly losing money in gambling without any restraint!

I saw Father's face with a bitter smile looking at me, the meaning of "Son, how have you changed?" shamed me into losing consciousness; Mother's moaning sound was responding to Father's bitter smile. Alas! My tears have run dry! Should I work hard to redeem myself?

Free Talk

A Realistic Understanding (Part 1)

— Shi Heng

When I explained the unreality of "Sanine," I mentioned that it was related to the author's artistic skill. Shortly after, I saw a criticism from a certain gentleman regarding my opinion. According to him, the reality of a character is determined by whether it actually exists, and has nothing to do with artistic skill. This conflict of opinions perhaps reveals a fundamental difference in our observations of art. For example, metaphorically speaking, in the case of creating characters, he views the function of art as a camera. No matter how skillful the photographer's technique, a real, existing person is always necessary. Conversely, I see art as the painter's brush, paints, and canvas. If a painter has a model in front of them, the object, though fixed in form, may not be reproduced exactly on the colored canvas. But if an image is born in the painter's mind, even if there is no actual model in front of them, their creation of a character can still be equally real. In short, I am opposed to viewing art as something overly mechanical.

That art cannot be said to be divorced from reality when it actually fulfills its artistic mission is indeed a principle. But this cannot lead to the conclusion that art must be a faithful reflection of reality. Because, for an artist or writer, the truthfulness of their creation does not lie in whether or not there is reality involved, but in the degree and accuracy of their understanding of reality, and how to concretely form their understanding into a work of art without destroying the integrity of the art. Therefore, the reality of art, or the reality that is transferred into art, is not merely an expression of the writer's general understanding of reality. The understanding must be profound and accurate, and the expression of that understanding must also be artistically accurate. To put it more clearly, the process of artistic creation has two steps: the first is the understanding of reality, and the second is artistic expression. What I previously referred to as "artistic skill" refers to the latter. If I have overlooked the importance of the first step and only valued the second step, then I should admit that I was wrong. But in fact, I have not done so. I said that "Sanine" has an exaggerated and inaccurate expression based on errors in the understanding of reality. Indeed, the reason why I criticize "Sanine" is because it has shortcomings in both of these aspects. Therefore, although I have not denied the first step, a certain gentleman clearly denies the second step, which cannot but be said to be his mistake.

It is easiest to prove this reason by comparing and examining Turgenev's "Fathers and Sons" and Artsybashev's "Sanine." Judging from the reactions that "Fathers and Sons" aroused in Russian society at the time of its publication, we cannot but doubt the truthfulness of the protagonist Bazarov. At that time, the older generation of fathers in Russia undoubtedly resented this type of person, while the younger generation of sons did not welcome him either, claiming that they were misrepresented. Both the old and the young relentlessly roared at the author of "Fathers and Sons," causing him to leave his homeland in tears, but he still stubbornly said, "Here is the prototype of a new era without any discount." Later, time proved that Turgenev's claim was not wrong. "Fathers and Sons," with its deep understanding of reality and its correct artistic expression, allowed this "prototype" to gradually grow. Eventually, people of the Bazarov type appeared in Russian society, and Bazarov himself was worthy of being a typical character.

On "Lying"

— Qu Yi

It is said that modern youth need to "lie." But some young people who like "simplicity" seem to be sighing again. Regarding this, I feel that I can only learn the tone of "Zhuangzi" and say: "Is the 'lying' of lying really lying? Is the 'truth' of truth really truth?"

I remember such a story: In a certain village, there were a father and son. In winter, they went to the mountain to chop firewood. Halfway through the work, the father sat on a stone and smoked. The son suddenly had a whim and thought of a question, so he asked: "Dad, do you think that at this time, the emperor must be using a golden axe to chop firewood on the royal mountain, right?" The father listened and scoffed. Then, he seriously said: "Nonsense, why would the emperor chop firewood? At this time, he must be sitting in front of the royal palace, in the sun, holding a golden pipe and smoking."

I think the father ridiculed his son's ideal of "the emperor using a golden axe to chop firewood" from the perspective of smoking, and pointed it out as nonsense; this is what the so-called "simple" youth now say is a precedent for modern youth to "lie." But in fact, the emperor is bound to hold a golden pipe and smoke, and will never take a golden axe to chop firewood. So the father's era was ultimately victorious. And simple youth can also stand on the front line.

However, I also remember Shun, the old emperor of China. Records of the Grand Historian, Basic Annals of the Five Emperors: "Shun plowed on Mount Li, and the people of Mount Li all yielded the boundaries; he fished in Lei Ze, and the people on Lei Ze all yielded their residences; he made pottery on the banks of the river, and the utensils on the banks of the river were all not badly made; in one year, the place where he lived became a settlement, in two years it became a town, and in three years it became a capital." Then Yao, under the tribal chief meeting, (see Shangshu "Consult the Four Mountains, I have been in office for seventy years," section) ceded the throne to Shun. After Shun became emperor, did he still "take a golden axe to chop firewood" and go farming and fishing? History has no clear statement, and it is not possible to speculate, but in light of the saying "The head rises, the workers flourish," the so-called Shun, who became emperor, was still participating in productive labor, and not just "sitting in front of the royal palace, in the sun, holding a golden pipe and smoking" to please himself, but that is a fact. Therefore, in the name of "being a person," the son's "lying" seems to be lovely. Perhaps this lie will turn into "truth."

However, precisely because this "lie" may become the truth, the "simple" youth have to stand up and scold the liar and advocate the so-called "philosophy of smoking." Moreover, the world is turbulent, everyone smokes, and cigarettes are attached with lottery tickets, and there is also an opportunity to get rich. If someone uses the words "the emperor must take a golden axe to chop firewood" again, there are few who will not be "pushed" or "kicked" by those who are good at smoking. And those who read "Zhuangzi," such as this humble little one, naturally have to shake their heads and sigh: "Is the 'truth' of truth really truth? Is the 'lying' of lying really lying?"

Impressions of Beiping

— Yao Ke

After the boy came to collect the tea money, the skyline of this ancient capital had already emerged far outside the train window. Under the strong sunlight, it looked like a shimmering piece, as ethereal as a dream, as hazy as a mist, not as majestic as described in the Beiping guide.

The train arrived at the station, and I squeezed through the crowd onto the platform. After a thorough inspection of the luggage, I squeezed out of the station on the platform again. Outside the station was a square, with dozens of rickshaws parked. "Coolies" with oily sweat on their faces were clamoring to come forward to solicit people squeezing out of the station gate. Two purple-faced policemen in yellow uniforms were waving rattan whips there to "maintain order," urging them to make way for "cars picking up lords and ladies." One car, two cars, three cars... the cars sped away from the station entrance, wrapping up a gust of dust like a thick fog, shrouding the square in front of the station. The remaining passengers without cars, the police, and the "coolies" struggled and wrangled in this dust.

I jumped into a rickshaw. In this man-made fog, the rickshaw puller pulled me out of the square. In front of me was the towering Zhengyang Gate. Looking at it in the dust, it seemed quite majestic, just saying that the city wall was more than three zhang high and five or six zhang wide; but somehow I only felt that it was listless, like a Vajra in a dilapidated temple.

× × × × × × ×

What is Beiping's impression on me? I can't say. Compared to the places I have been to, Beiping often reminds me of Suzhou in the south. On the surface, Beiping and Suzhou are simply not alike. From the perspective of color, Beiping belongs to rich and gorgeous, and Suzhou is plain. The roof tiles of Beiping have green, yellow, blue, and various other colors, the doors and windows are often vermilion lacquered, and women also love to wear bright red and green clothes; Suzhou is all black tiles and black lacquered walls, and women like plain attire. In terms of shape, Beiping is broad, and Suzhou is small and exquisite. The streets of Beiping need not be said, even a few large hutongs are wider than the main streets of Suzhou. In addition, of course, there are many places that are completely dissimilar, but these are only material differences.

In spirit, Beiping and Suzhou belong to the same category. The most obvious example is language. In the south, the most pleasant and playful is the "soft language of Wu" in Suzhou, and in the north, it is the "Beijing dialect" of Beiping. These two languages can be said to be "equally skilled" in terms of technique, both of which can roll on the tongue like lotus beads, and when listening carefully, they are the same, both containing a strong "feminine attraction." Aren't the ladies in the North-South social circles saying that they love a few words of Beijing dialect or Wu dialect?

Not only are the languages similar, but the atmosphere is also not different. Living in Beiping or Suzhou makes you feel so comfortable that your muscles and bones are numb. If you live in Beiping for three or two years, you will play with antiques, listen to Mei Lanfang, and feel that there is nothing else to do. In Suzhou, you will listen to storytellers, eat watermelon seeds, and feel that there is nothing else to do. When you speak Beijing dialect or Wu dialect fluently, you will understand what "pi sai" is, or what "Tang Bohu Points Autumn Fragrance" is. In addition, you will only shout "Menluocai" wildly in the theater, or spit a ground of watermelon seeds in the teahouse.

In short, Beiping is just an enlarged antique shop, and Suzhou is just an enlarged "Daoxiangcun."

I have only been to Beiping for less than two months, and I have not had the time to appreciate all the famous historical sites here one by one. Judging only from the places I have visited, there is really nothing new. Most of them have already been seen in photographs or paintings, and although the real scene is much larger than the one in the painting, it does not have the beauty in the painting. But when wandering in the Forbidden City, I seemed to feel a kind of flowing emotion rippling there, which was not present when looking at photographs and paintings. I looked with my eyes wide open 丨 丨

A glory that has lost its life is declining, declining there.

Huaqing Pool

— Qian Bai

"In the cold of spring, the Emperor bestows a bath at Huaqing Pool, the hot spring water smooths her creamy skin," what a fragrant and tender scene this is!

This Huaqing Pool is located in Lintong County, Shaanxi Province, a four-hour bus ride from Xi'an. Barren earthen forts, roads covered with gray sand, people with dark faces and hunger, and the air is so dull. From the outer contours, no one can believe that there would be a peerless beauty who "makes the beauties of the six palaces lose their color," leaving behind such romantic traces. However, history clearly tells us that there was such a miracle!

In order to preserve the ancient romance, someone recently renovated this Huaqing Pool. A main pool for water distribution was built under Mount Li, with an average water temperature of 104 degrees Fahrenheit. Two water distribution pools were also built, and water was distributed from the distribution pools to the East Pool, West Pool, Great Pool, and Concubine Pool. Bathing in the East Pool and West Pool is subject to a fee, and the price required is by no means affordable for ordinary people in Lintong. Therefore, there is a Great Pool to provide those who cannot afford the money with a bathing opportunity. Of course, if there is no distinction between levels, there will be many inconveniences. There is also the Concubine Pool, which is said to be the place where Yang Yuhuan washed her creamy body in those years. It is now for female guests to bathe in. Ordinary smelly men are of course not allowed to enter, so as not to offend the dignity of the Concubine.

We arrived here at around ten o'clock in the morning. Regardless of whether there is still the fragrance of Yuhuan left in the water, we always have to take a bath. Immersed in the pool built of cement and alum stone, thinking that when Yuhuan bathed here in those days, this pool may not have been as elaborate as it is now.

After leaving Huaqing Pool, everyone had the same feeling, that is, jumping into the hot spring to wash away the mud and dirt from the whole body. It was indeed very refreshing for a while, but after leaving here, it didn't take long for the whole body to be covered with mud and dirt again. Washing was equal to not washing. If you don't think that this is a historically famous site, you really want to shout "Oh no!"

Two Brothers (35)

— Guy de Maupassant, Translated by Li Weike

He looked up and saw, near the north, a deep and light gray shadow, which overwhelmed the sky and covered the sea, and was running towards them, as if it were a cloud falling from the sky.

He turned the boat around and, taking advantage of the tailwind, rushed straight to the embankment. The fog chased behind him and soon caught up. When it caught up with the Pearl, it surrounded her heavily, so thick that nothing could be seen; a chill passed through Pierre's limbs, as well as the smell of smoke and mold mixed together, a strange smell of sea fog, which made him close his mouth to avoid tasting this wet and cold dense cloud. When the boat returned to its original position near the dock, the whole city was already buried in this fine water vapor, which did not fall down, but moistened everything like rain, and slipped over the houses and streets like a flowing river.

Pierre, whose hands and feet were frozen, hurried home, fell on the bed, and wanted to take a nap before dinner. When he woke up and went to the dining room, his mother was saying to Jean:

"That aisle will be decorated very beautifully. We can put some flowers there. You see. I will take care of and change those flowers for you. If you have any banquets, this will look exceptionally gorgeous."

"What are you talking about?" the doctor asked.

"Talking about a very good house that I just rented for your brother. It's really not easy to find, a house located on the second floor, with doors to two streets. There are two living rooms, a glass-embedded corridor, a small circular dining room, this house is very beautiful for a boy to live in."

Pierre turned pale. A surge of anger choked his heart.

"Where is this house?" he asked.

"On Frangso I Avenue."

He had no more questions, he sat down, so enraged that he almost wanted to shout: "Is everything going to be his!"

His mother continued triumphantly:

"And think about it, I only spent two thousand eight hundred francs on the rent. This house was originally rented for three thousand francs a year, but I promised to rent it for three years, six years or nine years, so it's two hundred francs cheaper every year. Your brother will definitely be very happy living there. A lawyer will get rich as long as the house is beautiful. Because a beautiful house can attract customers, seduce them, keep them, make them respect, and make them know that the person living in such a house speaks naturally at a high price."

She was silent for a moment, and said again:

"We also have to find a house similar to this for you, which is naturally much simpler than this, because you have nothing, but it must also be quite lovely. I can assert that a suitable house is very useful for you."

Pierre replied nonchalantly:

"Ah! I, I will succeed by working hard and studying."

His mother stubbornly said:

"That's right, but I can assert that a beautiful house is very useful for you."

Halfway through the meal, he suddenly asked:

"How did you get to know him, this Maraisha?"

Brief Commentary

"Humor" and "Slapstick"

— Wei Ba

Private advocacy of "humor," public praise for "slapstick," these are two outlets for the pent-up frustration of ordinary people in "the face of national crisis," 丨 丨 in short, they are anesthetics.

Some say that it is certainly not good to be gloomy, and the production of humor has its own role, which is not wrong; but once a solemn matter is shrouded in the cloak of humor, it is difficult to see the truth of the facts clearly, and once it flows into the hands of slapstickers, there is only laughter. The harm it causes is generally similar.

For example, "capturing Japanese alive" is certainly a happy topic: but once performed by a clown, this meaning is no different from "capturing Zhang San alive." Similarly, "crying for Sun Yat-sen" is originally a very painful topic, but it is suitable to run straight to Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum and cry loudly, or hide at home and sob. If Wang Wu Neng and his like use the tune of "crying for Uncle Miao Gendu" and cry in a wailing voice, then the audience will intercept this tail of "entertainment technology" and leave behind the meaning of "crying." 丨 丨 In the eyes of the audience or listeners, Mr. Sun Yat-sen has also become "Uncle Miao Gendu II." This can be seen from the fact that in a survey of radio listeners, how many of them turned on the radio to commemorate Sun Yat-sen.

Therefore, "humor" is the language of slaves, and "slapstick" is only an ornament for after-dinner conversation in a prosperous age. If you want to find a way out from humor, and hear "patriotic thoughts" from a little tune, then you will be disappointed like looking for white cloth in a dye vat.

But what is the truth of the two? It lies in reducing the vitality of individual struggle and anesthesia!

Living in the modern situation, everyone has resentment, and everyone needs entertainment. The surge of life force forces people to rush forward to fight for the things they want to obtain. But when rushing, it is inevitable to knock down the other party or hurt yourself. Smart people will think of these things. Therefore, those who originally wanted to rush, did not rush, and expressed it as humor, quietly standing far away from the enemy with tears in their eyes and throwing a small stone, hoping to hit the target by chance, without being noticed 丨 丨 Because if they are noticed, even this right will be revoked, so smart people become even smarter. 丨 丨 What about those who are about to be rushed? They quickly stood up to reward slapstick, the purpose of which is to puncture the gathered resentment with a needle, hoping that everyone will laugh and temporarily forget the pain they are carrying. The method is originally very clever, and it is one step further than humor.

As for the so-called "promoting patriotic thoughts" and "advocating national spirit," in short, it is not worth a penny, it is just a "smokescreen."

Ward 20

— Yu Sheng

Nature is showing a smile to the world, the warm sunshine is shining on the earth, all the flowers are stretching out their buds, the leaves of the mulberry trees are also getting smaller and larger, the people on the road are showing a harmonious and youthful spirit, and the tourists in the parks are coming and going like weaving. The birds are jumping and chirping on the branches, and the breeze is softening all the idle people. This is the most joyful season of life... Spring!

The hospital is a first-class imperial hospital, and most of the patients are wealthy merchants and dignitaries. There are also poor people, who only come after all the hospitals have declared them hopeless. The patients living in the first- and second-class wards usually do not have serious illnesses, but the third-class wards are different. There are those who are terminally ill, and those who are poor and have no support, especially in that dark corner, the cold Ward 20, which has always been reserved for patients who have been declared hopeless by the doctor and are about to disappear from the world.

Old and sick, what a terrible encounter in life! An elderly patient, said to be seventy-four years old, lived in Ward 20. He had no relatives at all. Because he had no money, he could only occupy the dirtiest corner of the entire hospital.

He lay on the white bed, constantly groaning, his thin face covered with wrinkles that had suffered from wind and frost. From every line of deep-set, dark wrinkles, he had engraved the infinite suffering and trauma of his past life experiences. His head of white hair stood straight up, and you could see that in his shattered heart, the bitterness and indignation that filled his chest were burning like fire. When he occasionally moved, his legs trembled very badly, showing that his decaying limbs could not only carry his body, but also his sorrow. He was never seen smiling, his smile seemed to have been destroyed long ago, and he was never seen visiting him. It seemed that this poor old man had already been forgotten by mankind.

Without the doctor's permission, he often drank very strong yellow wine. This action clearly showed that he was eagerly hoping to quickly end his remaining life. When someone asked about his life, he always glared at the person like a madman, and immediately showed a nameless resentment that squeezed into his heart. The wrinkles on his face almost all twitched, his lips trembled, and blood-like hot tears flowed from his dry eyes. As a result, no one could be so cruel to ask any further!

When the nurse buttoned his clothes for him, he always shed tears of gratitude as if he had been touched by a concern, sometimes simply crying out loud. He felt sad about the pain of being helpless in his old age, the sorrow of being old, poor, and sick. Under the decay of life functions and the attack of all kinds of sorrows, the old man's condition became worse day by day.

One evening, when the nurse went to measure his temperature, she found him lying stiffly on the bed, his hands and feet were already cold, there seemed to be a little heat in his chest, and undried tears were still hanging on his face. The ragged clothes were piled up in 丨 piece, and a broken wine bottle was thrown on the ground.

He finally destroyed himself, and died like a dream after being drunk. People carried him into the "morgue," and the "philanthropist" gave him a coffin for his last rest. The ragged clothes still accompanied him to that unknown and vast world, but the yellow wine would no longer accompany him. There was no turmoil of relatives and friends mourning, nor the crying of children. The warm sunshine shone on his thin coffin, and he got rid of all the sorrows and pains of the world and rested quietly and forever.

Returning Home

— Bin Fu

Two Dollars and Ninety-Six Cents

After my teacher Mr. X's funeral, I went for a mountain outing with my older brother and my friend Mr. Li. To make a living, we rush about outside all year round, and we've been estranged from the scenery of the mountains and fields for a long time. Naturally, we wouldn't let this opportunity pass easily.

Although the sky was drizzling, our interest in visiting the mountains and forests did not diminish at all. In the morning, we chewed on many hot, steaming flatbreads (how delicious these flatbreads are, it's been many years since they touched my lips). Then, we rolled up our trousers, held up umbrellas, and walked out of the east gate.

The twenty-odd li walk didn't feel like much of a burden to us. The splashing raindrops didn't make us feel the slightest bit annoyed either. Perhaps we were tired of the city. We felt that the countryside truly had an indescribable sense of intimacy.

I can't say how much the scenery in the rain pleased our spirits. I think it would be more accurate to say that it increased our emotions more so than pleasure. At that time, we were standing on the seventh floor of a temple outside the east gate, gazing at the semi-circular horizon. We all unconsciously sank into memories. The unspoken silence lasted for several hours.

When we were panting as we walked down the stone steps one by one, we realized that it was past noon, and our stomachs were starting to demand food. So, we rushed into the city and randomly found a restaurant on the street.

I examined the decoration of the restaurant. Hanging on the walls were all Western paintings in glass frames. There weren't any Chinese-style calligraphy and painting screens. I felt like I was somewhere else, because I always thought that the shops in my hometown would usually hang screens and couplets of local elders. However, the hometown has changed. My mood is inevitably too old-fashioned.

In hunger, we devoured many dishes without knowing how much. The flavor of our hometown made the wanderers feel very appropriate, and we were intoxicated.

When we were paying the bill, we discovered that a small bowl of fried shrimp cost as much as 96 cents of silver dollars. We, who were unfamiliar with the prices, couldn't help but stare in astonishment. Later, according to the explanation of the shop assistant, we understood:

It turned out that not long ago, a clerk from a Shanghai bank came back to his hometown. He happened to order a bowl of fried shrimp at a restaurant. Unexpectedly, that day coincided with a wealthy family holding a wedding banquet, and all the shrimp in the city had been bought up. The restaurant couldn't fulfill the order, so the bank clerk became angry and decided to use "foreign money" to compete. The cook finally managed to get a small bowl of shrimp. The bank clerk felt he had face and rewarded him with 96 cents. From then on, the price of fried shrimp in our hometown was set at 96 cents.

I think that clerk who "benefited his fellow villagers" deserves to be praised, so I wrote it down as follows.

"Jianghu Art"

— Qiong Sheng

Among them, we single out the "Jianghu performers" who "make a living by selling skills." They beat gongs and drums in the streets and alleys, practice boxing, wield sticks, and perform some "tricks" to attract cheers from ignorant people, women and children, in order to earn money for food. We call this kind of life skill "Jianghu art."

The art of “Jianghu performers” becoming a life skill naturally has its unique and profound aspects. For example, they beat gongs and drums to gather spectators, making the noise as loud and grand as possible. The more spectators that are attracted, the better. Then, they deliver an eloquent opening speech, saying that they have traveled to the north and south capitals and all over the five lakes and four seas, to show that they have a deep origin and extraordinary background. They then brag about how they know the "kung fu" of thirty-six levels and the "changes" of seventy-two sets, to show how they have the ability to "steal the sky and change the day" and "reverse the universe". "The three religions and nine streams," they claim, "all belong to me." Needless to say, they speak eloquently and talk logically. After being "publicized", the spectators are happy to "open their wallets". This requires two or more people to "help out", with one blowing and the other praising, echoing each other, so that you are influenced and dazzled without realizing it. After the prelude is over, the main act begins. However, it is often not so easy. First, they need money. After all, the "tricks" are for the sake of money. Once the money is in hand, it may be a fully armed fight, with broadswords swinging and a fierce battle where you can't tell who's winning or losing. When the "war" is at its most intense, the "spectators" have to throw money. After the event, no matter who wins or loses, the two sides have already "reached an agreement", and the spectators throw money. Then, there may be unpredictable "illusions". Whether it is civil or military, it can be ugly or evil. Under the "clear sky and bright sun", many turtles, scorpions, snakes, and insects can be produced out of thin air. Whether the change is good or bad, because they can change, the "spectators" throw money. If the "spectators" are a little bored or annoyed, there must be stimulation. Suddenly, a child is beheaded, and a sharp blade enters the chest – it is a bloody tragedy. This can greatly intimidate. "Everyone has parents, and everyone has siblings." Where justice lies and where humanity is concerned, "if you have money, throw it, if you don't have money, throw it." You are not allowed to leave. When the money is gone and the bag is empty, the show is over. However, the "trick" is not over. It can be performed again at a different time and place.

However, "each trick has its own method, and each master has his own teaching." The "tricks" of this kind of "Jianghu art" can be performed falsely or truly. It can be performed in the sound of gongs and drums, or in the sound of cannons and bombs. It can be performed in the streets and alleys, or it can be performed on a larger scale, such as the province and the country. The size of the "trick" is different, and the amount of money the "spectators" throw is also different.

This kind of ability to speak eloquently, followed by gun and knife fights, ever-changing illusions, and killing and bloodshed to deceive "spectators" into throwing money is indeed a unique aspect of Chinese "Jianghu art." It still manages to coax ignorant people, women, and children into throwing money without complaining. Perhaps it is because its "publicity" is moving, the fighting is very good to watch, the changes are unpredictable, and the killing and bloodshed are truly shocking. Otherwise, it would be known as a scam and rejected. In fact, who doesn't know it is a scam? Knowing it and still being willing to bite the bullet and be fooled is either because the Chinese nation is easily deceived, or because it has its own inferior nature of slaves. This is indeed a matter that cannot be solved with all the thinking!

Modern Celebrity Calligraphy and Painting

Collaboration of Xiang Ning, Hong Wei, Man Qing, and Da Qian

Played, or the scope of the province and the country can also perform, the size of "tricks" different, "spectators" take money is different.

This kind of ability to say eloquent, followed by gun knife fighting, ever-changing, killing bloodshed to cheat "spectators" take money, is indeed a unique place in Chinese "Jianghu art". It is until now also coaxed a general ignorant people women and children take money without complaint, fear that it "propaganda" has a moving place, fighting is very good to look, change ghosts and gods unpredictable, and killing bloodshed is also really amazing, otherwise it will be known to be a scam and rejected. In fact, who does not know is a scam, knowing it and being willing to bite the bullet and be fooled, the reason is that the Chinese nation is easily deceived, or it has its own slave inferior nature, this is indeed a thing that can not be solved by all thinking!

Waking Up from a Dream

— Zu

Although I grew up in Shanghai, I often feel the boredom of life in this big city and curse it, because it has an atmosphere that makes people feel tired and irritable, attacking me powerfully. Therefore, I dream of going to the countryside, thinking of becoming a hardworking, leisurely, and happy farmer! At that time, I would climb trees to pick mulberry leaves to feed silkworms; personally take a hoe to cultivate seedlings, weed, and fertilize. In my spare time, I would happily read Tang poetry, taking poetry as my friend and using my own labor to solve my own livelihood. This is the most gratifying thing. And unexpectedly, be alarmed.

Moreover, there is no noise of paddlewheels, no glare of electric lights. There is no bragging, no flattery, no charming winks, no treacherous hearts or faces... What you see is green mountains, green water, the gurgling of springs, the chirping of birds, simplicity, and faithfulness... Ah! The vast beauty of nature!

But people in such an ideal and fulfilling place have all run to this city full of an atmosphere that makes people feel thin and irritable. This should surprise me to the utmost! I asked them, and they said that they plow in the spring and cultivate in the summer, harvest in the autumn and store in the winter, going out with a hoe under the stars and returning tired with the moon. They work hard all year round, exposed to rain and sun, steamed by heat and invaded by cold, without any rest. The farmwives manage the household, cook and mend clothes, and also carry babies on their backs to deliver food to the men in the fields. They keep the plum rains, pick mulberry leaves to raise silkworms, from picking cocoons to reeling silk and weaving silk, from planting cotton to spinning and weaving cloth, and also raise pigs and chickens, all of which are the work of the farmwives. But what is the result? Those who eat white rice from the bowl are not the farmers, and those who wear silk all over their bodies are not the silkworm-raising women. Not only that, but they also said that even though they plant the fields themselves, they are still not full. If this continues, they will undoubtedly become hungry ghosts! When I heard their words, I couldn't help but shudder. I woke up from my dream a little. Then, a few lines of poetry about depicting the suffering of farmers and silkworms flew into my memory:

"In February, they sell new silk, in May, the county slaughters new sheep; to cure the sores before your eyes, you cut out the flesh from your heart! Weeding the seedlings at high noon, sweat drips into the soil, who knows that every grain in the bowl is the result of hard work! Yesterday I entered the city, returning with tears in my eyes; those who wear silk, are not the silkworm raisers. Ninety-nine eighty-one, the poor man has finished his punishment: only then can he lie down to sleep, mosquitoes and fleas come out!"
