Novel

[Fragmented Memories of Childhood (10)>

— Lie Huo

Xiang Da was indeed Xiang Da, because he had herded cattle for three years, so he had learned a hundred or so mountain songs. He often argued with the cattle-herding children across the river. He won nine out of ten arguments. However, he showed me extra affection. Besides always sharing the fruit he stole from other people's back gardens with me, he also always took care of me, teaching me mountain songs. Sometimes I would also share some candy with him. All the candy was stolen from my mother's cupboard. My mother didn't give me much candy to eat in front of her. To eat candy, I had to steal it. Xiang Da ate the candy and said it was so sweet it went straight to his heart. From then on, he was even nicer to me.

After that, he taught me how to swim. He said he would first show me an example. So, he took off his shorts, did a somersault into the water, and swam two or three hundred times. I felt dizzy watching him. He also said that he was teaching me how to breathe underwater. As a result, I almost drowned in the water when I imitated him. He quickly pulled me out of the water, carried me to the hillside, and slapped my back with all his strength until I spat out a lot of water. After a long time, he said, "It's still not working. You have to use more strength!" As soon as I heard this sentence, I opened the cattle pen door. The yellow cow rushed out and almost knocked me down under its crotch.

I remember that although I was ten years old at that time, I wasn't as tall as the average ten-year-old child. If the yellow cow raised its head, I was only as tall as its lower jaw. Usually, I was five inches shorter than its spine. But this yellow cow was very kind. It didn't bully me because I was young. It just followed my short steps step by step under the restraint of the halter. Sometimes it showed a tired look and neighed a few times. If it stopped, you knew it must be defecating, otherwise it wouldn't do that.

I had already led the yellow cow out of the firewood gate, and my mother still rushed forward to urge me, "It's good enough to lead it to the hillside or the paddy fields to graze, but don't take it to the pond!" Naturally, the motive behind my mother's words wasn't the cow, but she was deeply afraid that I would play in the water and accidentally fall into the pond. There was no chance of coming back alive. The day before yesterday, He Xiazi gave me a fortune reading, saying that I had a water barrier in my life, especially in July, I had to be careful. My mother believed his words more than making a wish to the Bodhisattva of Mercy. She often said that he was a great fortune teller who answered every question and whose words were reliable, telling me not to play around, especially to be careful in July.

Not to mention my father and mother, even my eldest brother, who didn't get along with me very well, praised me, saying, "You never see any progress in your studies, but herding cattle is your specialty. The skinny yellow cow will get fat after you herd it for a few days. In the future, ask Dad to buy you a load of grain candy to eat!" This was a big talk that my eldest brother often said, and he seemed to have said it several times before. My eldest brother's words weren't very reliable, I understood in my heart, but I was also happy to hear these kinds of words.

After ten days, I met Xiang Da behind the mountain. He was also a cattle herder, but the cow he herded belonged to other people, not his own family's. He was two years older than me. When summer came, he wouldn't wear a shirt, sticking out his chest, bare skin, basking in the scorching sun. By the end of July, when most of the summer had passed, his skin would be tanned into a spicy sauce color with red inside black. Water would drip on it without leaving a trace, like mercury, it would disappear in a flash.

Movie Supplement

For Movie Criticism

— Li Fu

Recently, I have seen several articles on movie criticism. Some expressed dissatisfaction with the current formulaic, mechanized, and vulgar movie criticism, and some explained that what is most needed now is constructive criticism. Of course, the motivation of these words is to improve movie criticism and to promote Chinese movie culture. Following the transformation of the entire film industry, I think the proposal of this view and requirement is justified.

Sun Yu once said that movie criticism is a specialized subject, and critics must fully study criticism before they can point out whether the work is correct or not. Only in this way can the authority of the critic be established. At the same time, Fei Mu also said that critics have neglected the criticism of film techniques too much, so they have not been of much help to producers other than indicating consciousness. We admit that these are all essential admonitions to movie critics. Without sufficient knowledge of the film production process, movie critics will forever remain in the circle of conceptual criticism.

Yes, critics need to know the film production process, the overview and evolution of the film industry in various countries around the world, and the relationship between films and audiences. In other words, a very difficult and arduous task is placed before movie critics.

Undoubtedly, in order to fulfill the cultural mission of movie criticism, film critics should bravely take on this task. They should not regard rushing to see movies and rushing to write articles as their only duties. They should learn more from books, magazines, studios, and even movie theaters.

Here, for the sake of movie criticism, critics want to make some urgent hopes to all those who cooperate with the film industry.

After reading many conversations of artists, it is gratifying to know that they have already expressed a very friendly attitude towards critics. Here, we further hope that producers and critics will have further cooperation. In addition to books and magazines, critics also need a lot of practical materials, because their research, their exploration, and even their correct and scientific criticism, must have the supply of this practical information before they can be completed. You see when foreign film critics criticize a film, they not only criticize the entire work, but also analyze the composition of all the pictures, the length of each cut, and the number of words in the dialogue and subtitles, … and other substantial issues. I think that conscientious film artists, if they sincerely hope for the progress of Chinese cinema, will certainly not be stingy with this meaningful cooperation.

Film Review

"A Thousand Mile Fate" Review of The Man From Toronto

— Moore

In many literary criticisms in the past, it has been pointed out that British films and American films do not have absolutely different places in essence. Their difference is only a small difference in the way of expression. This argument, we now look at "A Thousand Mile Fate", has been more of an evidence.

"A Thousand Mile Fate" is nothing more than a dispute between men and women, and in this, even more serious events are not available. Some are just small comedies, and small storms, he mocked the man's seeing different thoughts, he mocked the girl's impatience, so!

In the current society in Europe and the United States, in addition to providing entertainment for gentlemen and serving them, movies are almost only a function of exerting techniques for all artists themselves. Therefore, they absolutely do not ask how meaningful the story is. They know that the story is simple and can command the technique as much as possible. They intentionally take this "small storm" and "small comedy" as the theme. Originally, they could do nothing but some small techniques.

In this "A Thousand Mile Fate", the director also completely focused on the fun, (the two words fun, in the past easy to make people recognize as funny jokes, in fact, can not adopt this narrow sense of understanding.) He is a scene, and then another scene, a shot after another shot, to describe what he wants to express, he is not afraid of trouble to narrate small things.

However, one point we admit that "A Thousand Mile Fate" is clever, is that no matter where, the director can always use all kinds of side lining to express the psychology of children. This is natural, because the director's life is determined by the environment, he is familiar with this place. Therefore, in this film, whether the male or female lead, can delicately express the children's "good tricks", curiosity, competitive, within and their weak will. The importance of this kind of life experience in local art is clearly illustrated. Especially our directors who want to shoot films for the farmers and workers, and the actors who want to perform the attitudes of the farmers and workers, should pay more attention to it!

The most ambitious masterpiece of Lionel Barrymore's life, "Who Toiled for Whom," will be screened in Nanjing.

Audience Comments

"Western Arabian Nights" After Viewing

— Shen Gong

In the modern film world, there is a cry for transformation, but there is a work like "Western Arabian Nights", which is a pity!

The naivete of consciousness is revealed in a white light and a black air, and the various absurdities are no less than the Journey to the West and the List of Gods and other kinds of gods and monsters. This is not only contrary to the purpose of film education, but also instills corrupt ideas into the minds of the general public, making the superstitious people more confused by the sayings of gods and monsters. I think this kind of work is really without the value of shooting.

In terms of performance, all kinds of deformed costumes have made me feel cold, and the great chieftain palace that the filming work boasts is simply a set of utensils for Taoists to do Taoist temples. Not only can it not show that it is the chieftain's palace, but it also reveals the director's shortcomings.

As for the poor performance of several word recruitments, it is even more annoying, even using both hands to slap on the subtitles, and after the trial screening does not modify, it is even more visible that this film is sloppy!

My Opinion on "Aladdin"

— Shi Chun

Indeed, "Arabian Nights" is a very interesting book, and the section of "The Story of the Magic Lamp" can especially arouse the interest of many people. But I think that making this story into a film is undoubtedly going to fail.

Even if you discard the consciousness, there are many absurdities that are overlooked by the director. For example, in the section where Aladdin dies, Aladdin is in the same place as a native, Aladdin dies and the native does not die, who would believe how the fire only burns Aladdin, and does not burn the native? There are many such improprieties, and at the end, the same old problems are revealed, and this kind of performance is far less than the description in the original book.

As for the actors in this kind of work that is not suitable for the times, it is impossible to please them in any way. Wang Chunyuan too much shows the attitude of a monster, and the palace lord played by Qian Siying seems like the characters said in the old novels, and the clothes also do not know what they are based on, there are many that are not Chinese and not Western.

In short, the film "Aladdin" is really a white fee and a thankless effort!

Charlie Chaplin Readies Himself Again

— Rowan

It has been a long time since we saw Charlie Chaplin's "City Lights," and he seemed like a figure weary of the silver screen. But now, suddenly, news of Charlie's re-emergence has come from Hollywood.

Charlie Chaplin is indeed a peculiar figure in Hollywood. He started his own Chaplin Film Company, writes his own scripts, directs himself, acts as the main actor, and produces his own films. He makes one or two films whenever he pleases, and when he is not pleased, he closes the doors and rests. This time, he has rested for two years and ten months.

What has Chaplin been doing during these two years of rest? During this long period of two years and ten months, he did not spend many days resting and doing nothing. He wrote at home every day. No one knows why, but he actually took up the life of a poor scholar, which most people find baffling.

Chaplin's long work of over two years has now been completed. The book is titled "A Retrospective of the Film Industry," and it has now been published by a major publisher in New York. After completing his work, Chaplin will take a short rest and then reorganize his old business. The doors of the Chaplin Film Company's studio will soon be open again.

This time, Chaplin will still be making a silent film, and like "City Lights," it will still abandon dialogue and intersperse it with other types of sounds.

News from the Club of Employees of Lianhua Factories One and Two

The second session of the supervisory and executive committees of the Lianhua Shanghai Factories One and Two Employees' Club was elected by the general assembly a few days ago. All film publications have carried the news. It is now learned that the said supervisory and executive committees held their first joint meeting at the club on October 3rd, and elected standing committee members and assigned work. The five standing committee members are Fei Mu, Sun Yu, Cai Chusheng, Wu Cun, and Tan Youliu, who will serve as ministers and secretaries of the General Affairs, Research, Organization, and Entertainment departments respectively. The four sections of the General Affairs Department, namely Social Affairs, Documentation, General Affairs, and Accounting, will be headed by Xing Shaomei, Zheng Junli, Miao Zhusan, and Nie Er respectively. The Registration and Investigation sections under the Organization Department will be headed by Wu Yonggang and Zhou Daming respectively. Of the three sections under the Research Department, namely Articles, Technology, and Editing, Technology will be handled by Pei Yiwei, while Fang Xue and Editing will be concurrently handled by Research Department Minister Sun Yu and Documentation Section Director Zheng Junli. The handover between the first and second sessions was completed on the 15th. At 7:00 PM on the afternoon of the 16th, the said supervisory and executive committees held their second joint meeting at the Club of Factory One, and passed several important proposals. Furthermore, in view of the slow progress and lax spirit of past work, it was decided to intensify work. The first Lianhua Employees' Grand Gathering will be held on December 2nd, and on the spot, Cai Chusheng, Nie Er, Wu Yonggang, Wu Cun, Jin Yan, Zheng Junli, and Xing Shaomei will be elected as seven members of the preparatory committee, responsible for General Affairs, Entertainment, Arrangements, Accounting, Fundraising, Documentation, and General Affairs. The preparatory committee is required to be established and produce all plans within this week to proceed.

Film Novel Woman's Weakness My Weakness (9)

— Fusheng

Ronald argued with him, "That won't do. You're a rich man now, not a newspaper boy anymore!" Illery said, "If I marry her, she won't necessarily still be a floor-scrubbing maid! Ronald, she's too good. No matter what you say! I'm determined to marry her." Ronald asked, "What about Chinny?" Illery said, "That's over. I don't even know why I liked her before. I don't understand why I listened to her. She's really a woman who strikes gold from men. Ronald, I notified the bank this morning to continue paying your allowance as before."

Ronald's allowance, his uncle had instructed the bank to continue paying! Wasn't that still Lolo's merit? Even if he didn't love her, he wouldn't forget her. How should he repay her? He should make her happy. Ronald was thinking when Lolo opened the door and came out. Illery exclaimed, "My little angel is here!" Lolo smiled slightly, weakly shaking her head and saying, "You two, please come to my room, I have something to say to you... Mr. Gregory, you are a kind and generous person, and I like you very much, but that's all. If I were the kind of woman who would marry you, think about it, how much better would I be than Chinny?" His head lowered, lost in regretful thought. Lolo took his hand and said, "You are truly a good man. Why don't you find someone closer to your age who truly loves you?" Illery raised his head and smiled at her, "Perhaps you're right, little baby. But I still hope you're wrong." Ronald laughed, "What she says makes a lot of sense."

Because Ronald was still smirking, Lolo turned around and said angrily to him, "You, you need reform ten times more than I do! I used to think that it was okay for a poor woman to marry a man for money and comfort. Now I know that's not enough. It's not enough for a man to just be good-looking. Take you for example, you could have been a good person, but you are too selfish and heartless. You are also the laziest. Why don't you work and do something for your uncle Illery? Even Gilat is better than you. As for myself, I am grateful for all the education you have given me in the past two months. I now understand everything about men. I don't want to marry any man anymore."

After Lolo finished speaking, she lowered her head again to tidy her clothes. She heard the sound of Illery walking out. She thought Ronald was also going to leave. But after waiting for a while, Ronald didn't leave. He said to Lolo, "Lolo, what you said about me needing to work is not wrong. I now beg you to take me as your personal slave. What do you say?" This seemed too good to be true. Lolo was a little skeptical, she was still tidying her clothes. Ronald said again, "During the day, I'll work in Illery's office. In the evening, I'll come back and work for you." Lolo still ignored him. He said again, "Lolo, why don't you use a useful young man? If you're willing to use me, I'll immediately hang up all your clothes for you!" All right, stop pretending, suddenly Lolo inexplicably found herself in Ronald's arms. (The End)
